অবশ্যই। তোমার লক্ষ্য যেহেতু **Python/Django Full Stack Developer হিসেবে আন্তর্জাতিক ক্লায়েন্ট ও কোম্পানিতে কাজ করা**, তাই আমি সাধারণ Spoken English নয়, **Developer-focused Spoken English Master Course** তৈরি করেছি।

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

## Beginner → Advanced → Professional

### 🎯 Course Goal

৬০ দিন শেষে তুমি পারবে:

* আত্মবিশ্বাসের সাথে ইংরেজিতে কথা বলতে
* বিদেশি ক্লায়েন্টের সাথে মিটিং করতে
* Job Interview দিতে
* অফিসে Professional Communication করতে
* Fiverr/Upwork Client-এর সাথে কথা বলতে
* Django/Python Project ইংরেজিতে Explain করতে

# 📅 আগামীকাল থেকে শুরু হবে **Day 1 – Spoken English Master Course**

**Day 1-এ আমরা শিখব:**

* কীভাবে ইংরেজিতে চিন্তা (Think in English) করতে হয়
* ইংরেজিতে কথা বলার ১০টি Golden Rules
* Greeting (Hello, Good Morning...)
* Self Introduction (Basic)
* ৫০+ দৈনন্দিন ব্যবহৃত বাক্য
* ৫টি বাস্তব Dialogues
* Pronunciation Tips
* Speaking Practice
* Homework ও Quiz

এই কোর্সটি আমি **একেবারে Beginner থেকে Professional Developer Communication** পর্যন্ত ধাপে ধাপে শেখাব।

------------------
# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# ✅ Day 1: Think in English + Basic Greetings + Self Introduction

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🧠 ইংরেজিতে চিন্তা করা (Think in English)
* 👋 Greeting শেখা
* 🙋 Self Introduction শেখা
* 💬 ৫০+ Daily Sentences
* 🎭 Real-life Dialogues
* 🔊 Pronunciation Tips
* 📝 Homework
* ✅ Quiz

---

## 🎯 Rule 1: বাংলা থেকে ইংরেজি অনুবাদ করা বন্ধ করো

অনেকেই মনে মনে এমন করে:

> বাংলা → ইংরেজি → বলা ❌

এতে কথা বলতে সময় লাগে।

এর পরিবর্তে:

> Idea → English → Speak ✅

---

### উদাহরণ

❌
"আমি পানি খাব"

বাংলায় ভাবলে:

আমি → পানি → খাব

তারপর ইংরেজি

I will drink water.

এভাবে সময় নষ্ট হয়।

---

### সরাসরি ইংরেজিতে ভাবো

Water...

I'm thirsty.

I need water.

I want water.

এইভাবে ভাবো।

---

## 🎯 Rule 2: ছোট বাক্যে কথা বলো

❌

Although I was tired...

✅

I'm tired.

I need some rest.

I'll sleep now.

ছোট বাক্য = Fluency বাড়ে।

---

## 🎯 Rule 3: প্রতিদিন জোরে জোরে বলো

Reading নয়।

Speaking.

কমপক্ষে

২০ মিনিট।

---

## 🎯 Rule 4: ভুল করতে ভয় পেয়ো না

Wrong English is better than No English.

---

## 🎯 Rule 5: প্রতিদিন একই বাক্য Repeat করো

কমপক্ষে

২০ বার।

---

## 📖 Greetings

## Morning

Good morning.

= শুভ সকাল।

---

## Afternoon

Good afternoon.

---

## Evening

Good evening.

---

## Night

Good night.

(ঘুমানোর আগে)

---

## Hello

সব সময় ব্যবহার করা যায়।

---

## Hi

বন্ধুদের জন্য।

---

## 📖 Greetings Reply

Good morning!

→ Good morning!

---

Hello!

→ Hello!

---

Hi!

→ Hi!

---

Nice to meet you.

→ Nice to meet you too.

---

How are you?

→ I'm fine.

---

## 📖 30 Most Common Greetings

| English           | বাংলা                             |
| ----------------- | --------------------------------- |
| Hello             | হ্যালো                            |
| Hi                | হাই                               |
| Good morning      | শুভ সকাল                          |
| Good afternoon    | শুভ অপরাহ্ন                       |
| Good evening      | শুভ সন্ধ্যা                       |
| Good night        | শুভরাত্রি                         |
| Welcome           | স্বাগতম                           |
| How are you?      | কেমন আছেন?                        |
| I'm fine.         | আমি ভালো আছি।                     |
| I'm great.        | আমি দারুণ আছি।                    |
| Nice to meet you. | আপনার সাথে পরিচিত হয়ে ভালো লাগল। |
| See you.          | পরে দেখা হবে।                     |
| See you soon.     | শীঘ্রই দেখা হবে।                  |
| Take care.        | নিজের খেয়াল রাখবেন।              |
| Have a nice day.  | আপনার দিনটি শুভ হোক।              |

---

## 100DaysOfCode  👤 Self Introduction (Basic)

### Model

Hello!

My name is Atiar Rahman.

I am from Bangladesh.

I live in Dhaka.

I am a Computer Science student.

I love programming.

I am learning Python and Django.

My goal is to become a Full Stack Developer.

Nice to meet you.

Thank you.

---

## 🗣️ Useful Daily Sentences (40)

## Morning

1. Good morning.
2. I just woke up.
3. I'm feeling great.
4. Let's start the day.
5. Have a nice day.

---

## Home

6. I'm hungry.

7. I'm thirsty.

8. I'm tired.

9. I'm sleepy.

10. I need water.

---

## School/University

11. I'm going to class.

12. The class has started.

13. The teacher is here.

14. I have homework.

15. Today's lesson is easy.

---

## Office

16. I'm busy.

17. I'm free now.

18. Let's work.

19. Please wait.

20. Thank you.

---

## Friends

21. How are you?

22. I'm good.

23. What's up?

24. Nothing much.

25. Let's go.

---

## Phone

26. Can you hear me?

27. Speak slowly.

28. Please repeat.

29. I'll call you later.

30. Goodbye.

---

## Shopping

31. How much is it?

32. It's expensive.

33. It's cheap.

34. I like this.

35. I'll buy it.

---

## Restaurant

36. I'd like some tea.

37. The food is delicious.

38. The bill, please.

39. Thank you.

40. Have a nice day.

---

## 🎭 Dialogue 1

A: Hello!

B: Hi!

A: How are you?

B: I'm fine.

A: Nice to meet you.

B: Nice to meet you too.

---

## 🎭 Dialogue 2

A: Good morning.

B: Good morning.

A: How's your day?

B: It's going well.

---

## 🎭 Dialogue 3

A: What's your name?

B: My name is Atiar.

A: Where are you from?

B: I'm from Bangladesh.

---

## 🎭 Dialogue 4

A: What do you do?

B: I'm a Computer Science student.

---

## 🎭 Dialogue 5

A: What are you learning?

B: I'm learning Python and Django.

---

## 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word        | উচ্চারণ (সহজভাবে) |
| ----------- | ----------------- |
| Hello       | হে-লো             |
| Morning     | মর-নিং            |
| Evening     | ইভ-নিং            |
| Python      | পাই-থন            |
| Django      | জ্যাঙ্গো          |
| Developer   | ডি-ভে-লপ-আর       |
| Student     | স্টু-ডেন্ট        |
| Programming | প্রো-গ্র্যামিং    |

> **পরামর্শ:** উচ্চারণ বাংলার মতো লিখে মনে রাখা শুরুতে সাহায্য করতে পারে, তবে ধীরে ধীরে ইংরেজি উচ্চারণ শুনে অনুশীলন করো।

---

## 🎯 Speaking Challenge

নিচের ১০টি বাক্য **জোরে জোরে ১০ বার** বলো।

1. Hello.
2. Good morning.
3. How are you?
4. I'm fine.
5. My name is Atiar Rahman.
6. I'm from Bangladesh.
7. I am learning Python.
8. I am learning Django.
9. I want to speak English fluently.
10. Thank you.

---

## 📝 Homework

## Part 1: নিজের পরিচয় লিখো (৮–১০টি বাক্য)

এই বিষয়গুলো অন্তর্ভুক্ত করো:

* Name
* Country
* City
* Education
* Skills
* Goal
* Hobby

---

## Part 2: মুখে বলার অনুশীলন

আয়নার সামনে দাঁড়িয়ে **২ মিনিট** নিজের পরিচয় ইংরেজিতে বলো।

---

## Part 3: Vocabulary

আজকের ২০টি গুরুত্বপূর্ণ শব্দ মুখস্থ করো:

1. Hello
2. Morning
3. Evening
4. Night
5. Name
6. Country
7. City
8. Student
9. Teacher
10. Friend
11. Learn
12. Speak
13. Listen
14. Read
15. Write
16. Programming
17. Python
18. Django
19. Developer
20. Goal

---

### ✅ Mini Quiz

**1. "কেমন আছেন?" এর ইংরেজি কী?**

A. Who are you?

B. How are you?

C. Where are you?

---

**2. "আমার নাম আতিয়ার।"**

A. I am Atiar.

B. My name is Atiar.

C. Both A and B (দুটিই সঠিক, তবে পরিচয়ের সময় **"My name is..."** বেশি স্বাভাবিক।)

---

**3. "আমি বাংলাদেশ থেকে এসেছি।"**

A. I from Bangladesh.

B. I am from Bangladesh.

C. I is from Bangladesh.

---

**4. "আপনার সাথে পরিচিত হয়ে ভালো লাগল।"**

A. Nice to meet you.

B. See you.

C. Good night.

---

## 🌟 Daily Mission

আজ অন্তত **৩০ মিনিট** শুধু ইংরেজিতে ভাবার চেষ্টা করো।

যেমন:

* *I'm hungry.*
* *I need water.*
* *I'm studying now.*
* *I have class today.*
* *I need to practice English.*

এগুলো বারবার মনে মনে বলো।

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# ✅ Day 2: Advanced Self Introduction + Family + Education + City & Country

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 👤 Advanced Self Introduction
* 👨‍👩‍👧 Family Introduction

## 🎯 Lesson 1: Advanced Self Introduction

### 📖 Model Self Introduction (Student)

> Hello!
> My name is **Md. Atiar Rahman**.
> I am from **Bangladesh**.
> I live in **Dhaka**.
> I am a **Computer Science student**.
> I am passionate about programming and web development.
> Currently, I am learning **Python, Django, Django REST Framework, React, and Machine Learning**.
> My goal is to become a **Full Stack Developer** and work for an international software company.
> In my free time, I enjoy learning new technologies and building projects.
> Thank you for listening.

---

## 🎯 Lesson 2: Introducing Your Family

### Vocabulary

| English | বাংলা    |
| ------- | -------- |
| Father  | বাবা     |
| Mother  | মা       |
| Brother | ভাই      |
| Sister  | বোন      |
| Family  | পরিবার   |
| Parents | বাবা-মা  |
| Married | বিবাহিত  |
| Single  | অবিবাহিত |

---

### Example

> There are **five members** in my family.

আমার পরিবারে পাঁচজন সদস্য আছে।

---

> My father is a businessman.

আমার বাবা একজন ব্যবসায়ী।

---

> My mother is a homemaker.

আমার মা একজন গৃহিণী।

---

> I have one brother.

আমার এক ভাই আছে।

---

> We are a happy family.

আমরা একটি সুখী পরিবার।

---

## 🎯 Lesson 3: Talking About Your Country

### Example

> I am from Bangladesh.

আমি বাংলাদেশ থেকে এসেছি।

---

> Bangladesh is a beautiful country.

বাংলাদেশ একটি সুন্দর দেশ।

---

> The capital of Bangladesh is Dhaka.

বাংলাদেশের রাজধানী ঢাকা।

---

> Bengali is our national language.

বাংলা আমাদের জাতীয় ভাষা।

---

> I love my country.

আমি আমার দেশকে ভালোবাসি।

---

## 🎯 Lesson 4: Talking About Your City

### Example

> I live in Dhaka.

আমি ঢাকায় থাকি।

---

> Dhaka is a busy city.

ঢাকা একটি ব্যস্ত শহর।

---

> There are many universities in Dhaka.

ঢাকায় অনেক বিশ্ববিদ্যালয় আছে।

---

> I like living here.

আমি এখানে থাকতে পছন্দ করি।

---

## 🎯 Lesson 5: Talking About Education

### Useful Sentences

I am a student.

আমি একজন ছাত্র।

---

I study Computer Science.

আমি কম্পিউটার সায়েন্স পড়ি।

---

I study at university.

আমি বিশ্ববিদ্যালয়ে পড়ি।

---

I enjoy learning programming.

আমি প্রোগ্রামিং শিখতে পছন্দ করি।

---

My favorite subject is Machine Learning.

আমার প্রিয় বিষয় Machine Learning।

---

I want to improve my English.

আমি আমার ইংরেজি উন্নত করতে চাই।

---

## 📚 50 Daily Speaking Sentences

### Self

1. My name is Atiar.
2. I am 22 years old.

6. I study Computer Science.
7. I love programming.

### Family

17. We eat dinner together.
18. My family supports me.

### Education

22. I attend classes regularly.
23. I complete my assignments.

25. I learn something new every day.
26. I ask questions in class.
27. My teachers are helpful.
28. I like studying with friends.
29. I read books every day.
30. Education is important.

---

### Country & City

31. Bangladesh is beautiful.
32. Dhaka is a large city.
33. The traffic is heavy.
34. The people are friendly.
35. I love my country.
36. I enjoy traveling.
37. I like visiting new places.
38. My city is growing.
39. I want to travel abroad.
40. I want to work internationally.

---

### Goals

41. I want to improve my English.
42. I practice speaking every day.
43. I never give up.
44. I believe in hard work.
45. I enjoy learning.
46. My dream is big.
47. I will achieve my goals.
48. I am improving every day.
49. I am confident.
50. I can do it.

## 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Self Introduction

**A:** Hello! What's your name?

**B:** My name is Atiar Rahman.

**A:** Where are you from?

**B:** I'm from Bangladesh.

**A:** What do you do?

**B:** I'm a Computer Science student.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Education

**A:** What are you studying?

**B:** I'm studying Computer Science.

**A:** What's your favorite subject?

**B:** My favorite subject is Machine Learning.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Goals

**A:** What do you want to become?

**B:** I want to become a Full Stack Developer.

**A:** Why?

**B:** Because I enjoy building software and solving real-world problems.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Family

**A:** How many people are there in your family?

**B:** There are five people in my family.

**A:** Tell me about your parents.

**B:** My father is a businessman, and my mother is a homemaker.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Country

**A:** Where do you live?

**B:** I live in Dhaka.

**A:** How do you like your city?

**B:** It's busy, but I like it because there are many opportunities.

---

| Goal        | গোল                |

---

> Hello! My name is Md. Atiar Rahman. I am from Bangladesh. I live in Dhaka. I am a Computer Science student. I am learning Python, Django, and React. My goal is to become a Full Stack Developer. Thank you.

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# ✅ Day 3: Talking About Your Daily Routine

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* ⏰ Daily Routine সম্পর্কে ইংরেজিতে কথা বলা
* 🕒 Time Expressions শেখা
* 🌅 Morning থেকে 🌙 Night পর্যন্ত Conversation
* 💬 60+ Daily Sentences
* 🎭 Real-life Dialogues
* 🔊 Pronunciation Tips
* 📝 Homework
* ✅ Quiz

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Daily Routine কী?

**Daily Routine** = প্রতিদিনের কাজের বর্ণনা।

এখানে সাধারণত **Simple Present Tense** ব্যবহার করা হয়।

### Formula

**Subject + Verb (V1 / V1+s/es)**

**Examples:**

* I wake up at 6 a.m.
* I brush my teeth.
* I go to university.
* I study English every day.

---

# 🕒 Lesson 2: Time Expressions

| English          | বাংলা     |
| ---------------- | --------- |
| Early morning    | ভোরে      |
| In the morning   | সকালে     |
| At noon          | দুপুরে    |
| In the afternoon | বিকেলে    |
| In the evening   | সন্ধ্যায় |
| At night         | রাতে      |
| Every day        | প্রতিদিন  |
| Usually          | সাধারণত   |
| Always           | সবসময়    |
| Sometimes        | কখনও কখনও |
| Often            | প্রায়ই   |
| Never            | কখনও না   |

---

# 🌅 Morning Routine

### Model

> I wake up at 6 o'clock.
> I brush my teeth.
> I wash my face.
> I take a shower.
> I have breakfast.
> I get ready for university.

---

### Useful Sentences

1. I wake up early.
2. I make my bed.
3. I brush my teeth.
4. I wash my face.
5. I take a shower.
6. I get dressed.
7. I comb my hair.
8. I have breakfast.
9. I drink tea.
10. I leave home.

---

# 🏫 University Routine

11. I go to university.
12. I attend classes.
13. I listen to my teachers.
14. I take notes.
15. I ask questions.
16. I study with my friends.
17. I eat lunch.
18. I visit the library.
19. I complete my assignments.
20. I come back home.

---

# 💻 Study Routine

21. I study Python.
22. I practice Django.
23. I write code.
24. I solve problems.
25. I read documentation.
26. I watch tutorials.
27. I practice English.
28. I revise my lessons.
29. I complete my tasks.
30. I learn something new every day.

---

# 🌙 Evening & Night Routine

31. I have dinner.
32. I spend time with my family.
33. I watch YouTube.
34. I read a book.
35. I review my notes.
36. I prepare for tomorrow.
37. I set my alarm.
38. I go to bed.
39. I sleep at 11 p.m.
40. I sleep well.

---

# 🎯 Useful Expressions

41. I usually wake up at 6 a.m.
42. I always eat breakfast.
43. I often study at night.
44. I sometimes watch movies.
45. I never skip my classes.
46. I enjoy learning every day.
47. I stay focused.
48. I try my best.
49. I manage my time well.
50. I am improving every day.

---

# 💬 Daily Conversation Sentences

51. What time do you wake up?

➡️ I wake up at 6 a.m.

---

52. What do you do after breakfast?

➡️ I go to university.

---

53. When do you study English?

➡️ I study English in the evening.

---

54. Do you exercise?

➡️ Yes, I do. / No, I don't.

---

55. What time do you sleep?

➡️ I usually sleep at 11 p.m.

---

56. How do you spend your free time?

➡️ I read books and practice coding.

---

57. What do you do after class?

➡️ I go home and complete my assignments.

---

58. Do you use your phone a lot?

➡️ I try to use it only when necessary.

---

59. What do you learn every day?

➡️ I learn Python, Django, and English.

---

60. Are you busy every day?

➡️ Yes, but I enjoy being productive.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Morning

**A:** What time do you wake up?

**B:** I wake up at 6 a.m.

**A:** What do you do first?

**B:** I brush my teeth and wash my face.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – University

**A:** Where do you study?

**B:** I study at university.

**A:** What's your major?

**B:** Computer Science.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Study

**A:** What do you study every day?

**B:** I study Python, Django, and English.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Evening

**A:** What do you do after dinner?

**B:** I revise my lessons and practice coding.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Night

**A:** What time do you go to bed?

**B:** I usually go to bed at 11 p.m.

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word          | Easy Pronunciation |
| ------------- | ------------------ |
| Routine       | রু-টিন             |
| Breakfast     | ব্রেক-ফাস্ট        |
| University    | ইউ-নি-ভার-সি-টি    |
| Assignment    | অ্যা-সাইন-মেন্ট    |
| Documentation | ডক-ইউ-মেন-টেই-শন   |
| Productive    | প্রো-ডাক-টিভ       |
| Practice      | প্র্যাক-টিস        |
| Alarm         | আ-লার্ম            |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips

**"Usually", "Always", "Often", "Sometimes", "Never"** ব্যবহার করলে তোমার কথা আরও স্বাভাবিক শোনাবে।

**উদাহরণ:**

* I usually study at night.
* I always complete my work.
* I often practice English.
* I sometimes play games.
* I never waste my time.

---

# 🗣️ Speaking Challenge

নিচের Routine-টি **৫ বার** জোরে জোরে বলো।

> I wake up at 6 a.m. I brush my teeth and take a shower. I have breakfast and go to university. I attend my classes and study Computer Science. In the evening, I practice Python, Django, and English. I go to bed at 11 p.m.

---

### 1. "আমি সকাল ৬টায় ঘুম থেকে উঠি।"

A. I wake up at 6 a.m.

B. I waking up at 6 a.m.

C. I wake at 6 morning.

---

### 2. "আমি প্রতিদিন বিশ্ববিদ্যালয়ে যাই।"

B. I goes to university.

C. I am go university.

আজ অন্তত **৫ মিনিট** আয়নার সামনে দাঁড়িয়ে **তোমার Daily Routine** ইংরেজিতে বলো।

উদাহরণ:

* I wake up at 6 a.m.
* I have breakfast.
* I go to university.
* I study Computer Science.
* I practice Python and Django.
* I practice English every day.
* I go to bed at 11 p.m.

**লক্ষ্য:** মুখস্থ করা নয়, নিজের জীবন সম্পর্কে স্বাভাবিকভাবে বলতে শেখা।

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# ✅ Day 4: Asking Questions Naturally (WH Questions + Yes/No Questions)

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* ❓ কীভাবে স্বাভাবিকভাবে প্রশ্ন করতে হয়
* 🗣️ WH Questions (What, Where, When, Why, Who, Which, Whose, How)
* ✅ Yes/No Questions
* 💬 70+ Daily Question Sentences
* 🎭 Real-life Dialogues
* 🔊 Pronunciation Tips
* 📝 Homework
* ✅ Quiz

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: প্রশ্ন করার মূল নিয়ম

ইংরেজিতে প্রশ্ন দুই ধরনের:

### 1. WH Questions

উত্তর শুধু **Yes/No** নয়, বিস্তারিত হয়।

উদাহরণ:

* What is your name?
* Where do you live?
* Why are you late?

---

### 2. Yes/No Questions

উত্তর সাধারণত:

* Yes, I do.
* No, I don't.

---

# 📖 Lesson 2: WH Words

| WH Word | Meaning     | Example                 |
| ------- | ----------- | ----------------------- |
| What    | কী          | What is your name?      |
| Where   | কোথায়      | Where do you live?      |
| When    | কখন         | When do you study?      |
| Why     | কেন         | Why are you happy?      |
| Who     | কে          | Who is your teacher?    |
| Which   | কোনটি       | Which book do you like? |
| Whose   | কার         | Whose bag is this?      |
| How     | কীভাবে/কেমন | How are you?            |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Question Structure

## ✅ Be Verb (am, is, are, was, were)

**Be + Subject + ...?**

Examples:

* Are you ready?
* Is he busy?
* Were they at home?

---

## ✅ Do/Does

**Do/Does + Subject + V1?**

Examples:

* Do you like coffee?
* Does she play football?
* Do they study English?

---

## ✅ Did

**Did + Subject + V1?**

Examples:

* Did you call me?
* Did he finish the work?

---

## ✅ Modal Verbs

**Can/Will/Should/May + Subject + V1?**

Examples:

* Can you help me?
* Will you come?
* Should I wait?

---

# 💬 20 WH Question Examples

### What

1. What is your name?
2. What do you do?
3. What are you learning?
4. What is your hobby?
5. What is your favorite food?

---

### Where

6. Where do you live?
7. Where are you going?
8. Where do you study?
9. Where is your office?
10. Where did you buy it?

---

### When

11. When do you wake up?
12. When is your class?
13. When will you come?
14. When did you start learning English?
15. When do you exercise?

---

### Why

16. Why are you smiling?
17. Why do you like Python?
18. Why are you late?
19. Why did you call me?
20. Why are you learning English?

---

# 👤 About Yourself

21. What is your full name?

22. How old are you?

23. Where are you from?

24. What do you study?

25. What is your goal?

# 🎓 Education

27. Who is your favorite teacher?

29. Why do you like programming?

30. When do you study?

---

# 💻 Programming

32. Why are you learning Python?

33. Do you know Django?

34. Can you build websites?

35. What projects are you working on?

---

# 🏠 Daily Life

36. Do you cook?

37. Do you drink tea?

38. Do you exercise?

39. Do you watch movies?

40. Do you read books?

---

# 👨‍👩‍👧 Family

41. How many people are there in your family?

42. Who is the oldest in your family?

43. Do you live with your parents?

44. What does your father do?

45. What does your mother do?

---

# 💬 Yes/No Questions

46. Are you busy?

47. Is your friend here?

48. Do you speak English?

49. Does your brother work?

50. Did you finish your homework?

51. Can you swim?

52. Can you drive?

53. Will you come tomorrow?

54. Should I call you?

55. May I come in?

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Meeting Someone

**A:** Hello!

**B:** Hi!

**A:** What's your name?

**B:** My name is Atiar.

**A:** Where are you from?

**B:** I'm from Bangladesh.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Education

**A:** What do you study?

**B:** I study Computer Science.

**A:** Why do you like it?

**B:** Because I enjoy solving problems.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Programming

**A:** What programming language are you learning?

**B:** I'm learning Python.

**A:** Why Python?

**B:** Because it's easy to learn and very powerful.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Daily Routine

**A:** When do you wake up?

**B:** I wake up at 6 a.m.

**A:** Do you exercise?

**B:** Yes, I do.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Future Plan

**A:** What do you want to become?

**B:** I want to become a Full Stack Developer.

**A:** Why?

**B:** Because I love building software.

| Because     | বি-কজ              |
| Favorite    | ফে-ভা-রিট          |
| Programming | প্রো-গ্র্যামিং     |
| Language    | ল্যাং-গুয়েজ       |
| Powerful    | পাওয়ার-ফুল        |
| Problem     | প্রব-লেম           |

❌ Bangladesh.

✅ I am from Bangladesh.

---

❌ Python.

✅ I am learning Python.

---

❌ Student.

✅ I am a Computer Science student.

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. "তোমার নাম কী?"

A. What your name?

B. What is your name?

C. Where is your name?

---

### 2. "তুমি কোথায় থাকো?"

A. Where do you live?

B. Where you live?

C. Where are live?

---

### 3. "তুমি কি Python শিখছ?"

A. Do you learning Python?

B. Are you learning Python?

C. You learning Python?

---

### 4. "তুমি কি আমাকে সাহায্য করতে পারবে?"

A. Can you help me?

B. Do you can help me?

C. Can help me you?

---

### 5. "তুমি কেন ইংরেজি শিখছ?"

A. Why do you learn English?

B. Why are you learning English?

C. Both A and B are correct, but **B** is better when talking about your current learning journey.

---

# 🌟 Daily Mission

আজ অন্তত **১৫টি প্রশ্ন** নিজেকে ইংরেজিতে করো এবং **সম্পূর্ণ বাক্যে উত্তর দাও**।

উদাহরণ:

* What is my goal?

* My goal is to become a Full Stack Developer.

* Why am I learning English?

* I am learning English to communicate confidently with international clients.

এভাবে প্রশ্ন–উত্তর অনুশীলন করলে খুব দ্রুত ইংরেজিতে ভাবা ও কথা বলার দক্ষতা বাড়বে।

---

# 📅 আগামীকাল (Day 5)

আমরা শিখব:

* ❤️ Talking About Hobbies & Interests
* 👍 Likes and Dislikes
* 🎯 Talking About Goals and Dreams
* 💬 70+ Useful Speaking Sentences
* 🎭 Real-life Conversations
* 📝 Homework & Quiz

-----





# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# ✅ Day 5: Talking About Hobbies, Interests, Likes & Dislikes

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* ❤️ Hobbies সম্পর্কে ইংরেজিতে কথা বলা
* 👍 Likes & Dislikes প্রকাশ করা
* 🎯 Goals & Dreams নিয়ে কথা বলা
* 💬 70+ Useful Daily Sentences
* 🎭 Real-life Dialogues
* 🔊 Pronunciation Tips
* 📝 Homework
* ✅ Quiz

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Hobby কী?

**Hobby** = অবসর সময়ে আনন্দের জন্য করা কাজ।

### সাধারণ Hobbies

| English            | বাংলা       |
| ------------------ | ----------- |
| Reading books      | বই পড়া     |
| Playing football   | ফুটবল খেলা  |
| Programming        | প্রোগ্রামিং |
| Watching movies    | সিনেমা দেখা |
| Listening to music | গান শোনা    |
| Traveling          | ভ্রমণ       |
| Photography        | ছবি তোলা    |
| Cooking            | রান্না      |
| Gardening          | বাগান করা   |
| Drawing            | আঁকা        |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Talking About Your Hobbies

### Examples

> My hobby is programming.

আমার শখ প্রোগ্রামিং।

---

> I enjoy reading books.

আমি বই পড়তে উপভোগ করি।

---

> I like solving programming problems.

আমি প্রোগ্রামিং সমস্যা সমাধান করতে পছন্দ করি।

---

> I spend my free time learning new technologies.

আমি অবসর সময়ে নতুন প্রযুক্তি শিখি।

---

> Coding is my favorite hobby.

কোডিং আমার প্রিয় শখ।

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Talking About Likes

### Useful Patterns

* I like...
* I love...
* I enjoy...
* I'm interested in...
* My favorite... is...

### Examples

* I like Python.
* I love web development.
* I enjoy learning English.
* I'm interested in Artificial Intelligence.
* My favorite subject is Machine Learning.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: Talking About Dislikes

### Useful Patterns

* I don't like...
* I dislike...
* I hate... *(শুধু খুব শক্তিশালী অপছন্দ বোঝাতে ব্যবহার করো)*
* I'm not interested in...

### Examples

* I don't like wasting time.
* I dislike dishonesty.
* I'm not interested in gossip.
* I don't like spicy food.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 5: Talking About Goals & Dreams

### Useful Sentences

* My dream is to become a software engineer.
* My goal is to work for an international company.
* I want to improve my English.
* I want to build useful software.
* I hope to travel around the world.
* I believe hard work leads to success.

---

# 💬 70 Daily Speaking Sentences

## Hobbies

1. My hobby is programming.
2. I enjoy coding.
3. I like reading books.
4. I love learning new skills.
5. I watch educational videos.
6. I practice English every day.
7. I solve coding problems.
8. I enjoy building projects.
9. I write code in my free time.
10. Learning makes me happy.

---

## Likes

11. I like coffee.
12. I love tea.
13. I enjoy traveling.
14. I like helping people.
15. I enjoy teamwork.
16. I like learning languages.
17. I love technology.
18. I enjoy challenges.
19. I like clean environments.
20. I enjoy meeting new people.

---

## Dislikes

21. I don't like noise.
22. I don't like wasting time.
23. I dislike laziness.
24. I don't like being late.
25. I dislike negative thinking.
26. I don't like unhealthy food.
27. I avoid unnecessary arguments.
28. I don't like dishonesty.
29. I dislike distractions while studying.
30. I don't like giving up.

---

## Goals

31. I want to become a Full Stack Developer.
32. I want to improve my communication skills.
33. I want to work abroad.
34. I want to help my family.
35. I want to build successful products.
36. My goal is to become financially independent.
37. I want to start my own company someday.
38. I dream of working with international clients.
39. I believe in continuous learning.
40. I never stop improving.

---

## Personality

41. I am hardworking.
42. I am honest.
43. I am friendly.
44. I am curious.
45. I like learning from my mistakes.
46. I stay positive.
47. I work every day to improve.
48. I enjoy solving real-world problems.
49. I believe practice is the key to success.
50. I try to be disciplined.

---

## Everyday Conversation

51. What is your hobby?

52. My hobby is programming.

53. What do you do in your free time?

54. I read books and practice coding.

55. What do you like most?

56. I like learning new technologies.

57. What do you dislike?

58. I don't like wasting time.

59. What is your dream?

60. My dream is to become a Full Stack Developer.

61. Why do you like programming?

62. Because I enjoy solving problems.

63. What motivates you?

64. Learning new things motivates me.

65. What do you usually do on weekends?

66. I study, practice coding, and spend time with my family.

67. What is your biggest goal?

68. To become an excellent software engineer.

69. Do you enjoy learning English?

70. Yes, I do. It helps me communicate with people around the world.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Hobbies

**A:** What's your hobby?

**B:** My hobby is programming.

**A:** Why do you like it?

**B:** Because I enjoy solving problems.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Free Time

**A:** What do you do in your free time?

**B:** I read books and practice coding.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Goals

**A:** What's your dream?

**B:** My dream is to become a Full Stack Developer.

**A:** Why?

**B:** Because I want to build useful software.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Likes

**A:** Do you like English?

**B:** Yes, I do.

**A:** Why?

**B:** Because it helps me communicate with international clients.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Weekend

**A:** What do you usually do on weekends?

**B:** I study programming, practice English, and work on personal projects.

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word        | Easy Pronunciation |
| ----------- | ------------------ |
| Hobby       | হবি                |
| Interest    | ইন-ট্রেস্ট         |
| Favorite    | ফে-ভা-রিট          |
| Technology  | টেক-নল-জি          |
| Discipline  | ডিস-সি-প্লিন       |
| Independent | ইন-ডি-পেন-ডেন্ট    |
| Challenge   | চ্যাল-এঞ্জ         |
| Motivation  | মো-টি-ভে-শন        |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips

শুধু **"I like..."** ব্যবহার না করে বিভিন্ন Expression ব্যবহার করো।

### Instead of:

❌ I like programming.

### Say:

✅ I really enjoy programming.

✅ Programming is my favorite hobby.

✅ I'm passionate about programming.

✅ I'm interested in software development.

---

# 🗣️ Speaking Challenge

নিচের পরিচয়টি **৫ বার** বলো।

> Hello! My hobby is programming. I enjoy building web applications with Python and Django. I also practice English every day because I want to communicate with international clients. My dream is to become a successful Full Stack Developer and build software that helps people.

---

আয়নার সামনে দাঁড়িয়ে **৩–৫ মিনিট** তোমার Hobby ও Goal সম্পর্কে ইংরেজিতে বলো।

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. "আমার শখ প্রোগ্রামিং।"

A. My hobby is programming.

B. My hobby programming.

C. I hobby programming.

---

### 2. "আমি নতুন প্রযুক্তি শিখতে ভালোবাসি।"

A. I love learning new technologies.

B. I love learn technology.

C. I loving technology.

---

### 3. "আমি সময় নষ্ট করতে পছন্দ করি না।"

A. I don't like wasting time.

B. I not like wasting time.

C. I don't wasting time.

---

### 4. "আমার লক্ষ্য একজন ফুল স্ট্যাক ডেভেলপার হওয়া।"

A. My goal is to become a Full Stack Developer.

B. My goal become Full Stack Developer.

C. My goal is Full Stack.

---

### 5. "আমি আন্তর্জাতিক ক্লায়েন্টদের সাথে কাজ করতে চাই।"

A. I want to work with international clients.

B. I want work international client.

C. I working international clients.

---

# 🌟 Daily Mission

আজ **৫ মিনিট** ধরে নিচের তিনটি প্রশ্নের উত্তর ইংরেজিতে বলো:

1. What is your hobby?
2. What do you like doing in your free time?
3. What is your biggest dream?

**লক্ষ্য:** মুখস্থ উত্তর নয়—নিজের বাস্তব জীবনের উত্তর দেওয়ার অভ্যাস গড়ে তোলা।

-------------
# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# ✅ Day 6: Talking About Time, Days, Months & Dates

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🕒 Time বলতে শেখা
* 📅 Days of the Week
* 📆 Months of the Year
* 📍 Date বলার নিয়ম
* ⏰ Asking & Telling the Time
* 💬 70+ Daily Sentences
* 🎭 Real-life Dialogues
* 📝 Homework
* ✅ Quiz

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Asking the Time

### সবচেয়ে সাধারণ প্রশ্ন

**What time is it?**
= এখন কয়টা বাজে?

---

**Do you have the time?**
= আপনার কাছে সময় আছে?

---

**Could you tell me the time, please?**
= দয়া করে সময়টা বলবেন?

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Telling the Time

### Examples

**It's 7:00.**
= সাতটা বাজে।

---

**It's 7:15.**
= সাতটা পনেরো।

---

**It's 7:30.**
= সাড়ে সাতটা।

---

**It's 7:45.**
= সাতটা পঁয়তাল্লিশ।

---

## ইংরেজিতে Natural Way

| Time | English                    |
| ---- | -------------------------- |
| 7:00 | It's seven o'clock.        |
| 7:05 | It's five past seven.      |
| 7:15 | It's a quarter past seven. |
| 7:30 | It's half past seven.      |
| 7:45 | It's a quarter to eight.   |
| 7:55 | It's five to eight.        |

> **মনে রাখো:** দৈনন্দিন কথায় "It's seven fifteen." বা "It's seven thirty." বললেও সম্পূর্ণ সঠিক।

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Days of the Week

| English   | বাংলা       |
| --------- | ----------- |
| Monday    | সোমবার      |
| Tuesday   | মঙ্গলবার    |
| Wednesday | বুধবার      |
| Thursday  | বৃহস্পতিবার |
| Friday    | শুক্রবার    |
| Saturday  | শনিবার      |
| Sunday    | রবিবার      |

---

### Examples

Today is Monday.

আজ সোমবার।

---

Tomorrow is Tuesday.

আগামীকাল মঙ্গলবার।

---

Yesterday was Sunday.

গতকাল রবিবার ছিল।

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: Months

| English   | বাংলা       |
| --------- | ----------- |
| January   | জানুয়ারি   |
| February  | ফেব্রুয়ারি |
| March     | মার্চ       |
| April     | এপ্রিল      |
| May       | মে          |
| June      | জুন         |
| July      | জুলাই       |
| August    | আগস্ট       |
| September | সেপ্টেম্বর  |
| October   | অক্টোবর     |
| November  | নভেম্বর     |
| December  | ডিসেম্বর    |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 5: Talking About Dates

### Examples

**Today is June 29.**

আজ ২৯ জুন।

---

**Today is June 29, 2026.**

আজ ২৯ জুন, ২০২৬।

---

**My birthday is on March 10.**

আমার জন্মদিন ১০ মার্চ।

---

### Date লেখার নিয়ম

* June 29, 2026 *(American style)*
* 29 June 2026 *(British style)*

---

# 🎯 Lesson 6: Talking About Schedules

### Examples

My class starts at 9 a.m.

আমার ক্লাস সকাল ৯টায় শুরু হয়।

---

The meeting is at 3 p.m.

মিটিং বিকেল ৩টায়।

---

I usually study at night.

আমি সাধারণত রাতে পড়ি।

---

I work from Monday to Friday.

আমি সোমবার থেকে শুক্রবার পর্যন্ত কাজ করি।

---

# 💬 70 Daily Speaking Sentences

## Time

1. What time is it?
2. It's 8 o'clock.
3. It's half past nine.
4. It's a quarter past ten.
5. It's a quarter to five.
6. It's almost noon.
7. It's midnight.
8. I'm late.
9. I'm on time.
10. Hurry up!

---

## Days

11. Today is Monday.
12. Tomorrow is Tuesday.
13. Yesterday was Sunday.
14. I study every Monday.
15. I don't work on Friday.
16. Saturday is my holiday.
17. Sunday is my favorite day.
18. I have an exam on Thursday.
19. We have a meeting on Wednesday.
20. I'll see you on Monday.

---

## Months

21. My birthday is in March.
22. We have holidays in December.
23. Summer starts in June.
24. I started learning English in January.
25. I will graduate next year.
26. July is usually hot.
27. February has 28 or 29 days.
28. October is a beautiful month.
29. November is busy for me.
30. August is very rainy.

---

## Schedule

31. My class starts at 9 a.m.
32. My class ends at 1 p.m.
33. I wake up at 6 a.m.
34. I have lunch at 2 p.m.
35. I go to bed at 11 p.m.
36. I study English every evening.
37. I practice coding every night.
38. I usually finish work by 6 p.m.
39. I have free time after dinner.
40. I plan my day every morning.

---

## Everyday Use

41. What time do you wake up?
42. I wake up at 6 a.m.
43. When is your class?
44. My class is at 10 a.m.
45. What day is today?
46. Today is Monday.
47. What's today's date?
48. Today is June 29.
49. Are you free tomorrow?
50. Yes, I am.

---

## More Useful Sentences

51. I'm available after 5 p.m.
52. Let's meet tomorrow.
53. I'll call you tonight.
54. See you next week.
55. I'm busy this afternoon.
56. I have a meeting this morning.
57. I arrived on time.
58. I missed the bus.
59. Don't be late.
60. Time is valuable.
61. I manage my time well.
62. Please be punctual.
63. The meeting starts in ten minutes.
64. I have a busy schedule today.
65. I'll finish it by tomorrow.
66. I have a deadline this Friday.
67. Let's meet at 4 p.m.
68. I need more time.
69. I'm free this weekend.
70. Have a great day!

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Asking the Time

**A:** What time is it?

**B:** It's 8:30.

**A:** Thanks!

**B:** You're welcome.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Class Schedule

**A:** When does your class start?

**B:** It starts at 9 a.m.

**A:** What time does it end?

**B:** It ends at 1 p.m.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Meeting

**A:** Are you free tomorrow?

**B:** Yes, I am.

**A:** Let's meet at 4 p.m.

**B:** Sounds good!

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Weekend

**A:** What are you doing this weekend?

**B:** I'm going to practice coding and English.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Birthday

**A:** When is your birthday?

**B:** My birthday is on March 10.

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word      | Easy Pronunciation           |
| --------- | ---------------------------- |
| Quarter   | কোয়ার-টার                   |
| Half      | হাফ                          |
| Schedule  | স্কে-জুল (US) / শেড-ইউল (UK) |
| Available | আ-ভেই-লা-বল                  |
| Deadline  | ডেড-লাইন                     |
| Punctual  | পাংক-চু-য়াল                 |
| Weekend   | উইক-এন্ড                     |
| Tomorrow  | টু-মরো                       |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips

সময় বলার সময় পুরো বাক্য ব্যবহার করো।

❌ 8:30.

✅ It's 8:30.

---

❌ Monday.

✅ Today is Monday.

---

❌ March.

✅ My birthday is in March.

---

# 🗣️ Speaking Challenge

নিচের প্রশ্নগুলোর উত্তর ইংরেজিতে বলো।

1. What time do you wake up?
2. What day is today?
3. What's today's date?
4. When is your English practice?
5. When is your birthday?
6. What time do you go to bed?
7. Are you free this weekend?
8. What do you do every Monday?
9. How do you manage your time?
10. What is your schedule today?

* I wake up at...
* My class starts at...
* I practice English at...
* I go to bed at...

---

## Part 2 – Speaking

৩ মিনিট ধরে তোমার **Daily Schedule** ইংরেজিতে বলো।

## Part 3 – Vocabulary (20 Words)

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. "এখন কয়টা বাজে?"

A. What time is it?

B. What is time?

C. Which time?

---

### 2. "আজ সোমবার।"

A. Today Monday.

B. Today is Monday.

C. It Monday.

---

### 3. "আমার ক্লাস সকাল ৯টায় শুরু হয়।"

A. My class starts at 9 a.m.

B. My class start 9.

C. My class is start at 9.

---

### 4. "আগামীকাল দেখা হবে।"

A. See you tomorrow.

B. Meet tomorrow you.

C. Tomorrow see.

---

### 5. "আমি সাধারণত রাত ১১টায় ঘুমাতে যাই।"

A. I usually go to bed at 11 p.m.

B. I usually go bed 11.

C. I go to sleep usually at 11 p.m. *(এটিও সঠিক, তবে A বেশি স্বাভাবিক ও প্রচলিত।)*

---

# 🌟 Daily Mission

আজ ১০ মিনিট ধরে **সময় ও তারিখ** নিয়ে ইংরেজিতে কথা বলার অনুশীলন করো।

উদাহরণ:

* Today is Monday.
* Today's date is June 29.
* I wake up at 6 a.m.
* My class starts at 9 a.m.
* I practice English every evening.
* I usually go to bed at 11 p.m.

---

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# ✅ Day 7: Talking About Weather & Seasons

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🌤️ আবহাওয়া (Weather) সম্পর্কে ইংরেজিতে কথা বলা
* 🌸 চারটি ঋতু (Seasons)
* ☀️ Sunny, 🌧️ Rainy, ☁️ Cloudy, 🌬️ Windy ইত্যাদি শব্দ শেখা
* 💬 70+ Daily Speaking Sentences
* 🎭 Real-life Dialogues
* 🔊 Pronunciation Tips
* 📝 Homework
* ✅ Quiz

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Weather Vocabulary

| English | বাংলা         |
| ------- | ------------- |
| Weather | আবহাওয়া      |
| Sunny   | রৌদ্রোজ্জ্বল  |
| Rainy   | বৃষ্টিময়     |
| Cloudy  | মেঘলা         |
| Windy   | বাতাসযুক্ত    |
| Hot     | গরম           |
| Cold    | ঠান্ডা        |
| Warm    | উষ্ণ          |
| Cool    | শীতল          |
| Humid   | আর্দ্র        |
| Stormy  | ঝড়ো          |
| Foggy   | কুয়াশাচ্ছন্ন |
| Snowy   | তুষারপূর্ণ    |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Asking About the Weather

### Common Questions

**How's the weather?**

= আবহাওয়া কেমন?

---

**What's the weather like today?**

= আজ আবহাওয়া কেমন?

---

**Is it raining?**

= কি বৃষ্টি হচ্ছে?

---

**Is it hot outside?**

= বাইরে কি গরম?

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Talking About the Weather

### Examples

It's sunny today.

আজ রোদ উঠেছে।

---

It's raining.

বৃষ্টি হচ্ছে।

---

It's cloudy today.

আজ আকাশ মেঘলা।

---

It's very hot today.

আজ খুব গরম।

---

It's cold this morning.

আজ সকালে ঠান্ডা।

---

There's a strong wind.

জোরে বাতাস বইছে।

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: Seasons

| Season        | বাংলা                        |
| ------------- | ---------------------------- |
| Spring        | বসন্ত                        |
| Summer        | গ্রীষ্ম                      |
| Autumn (Fall) | শরৎ (Fall – আমেরিকান ইংরেজি) |
| Winter        | শীত                          |

> অনেক দেশে **Rainy Season (বর্ষাকাল)** আলাদাভাবে বলা হয়, যদিও এটি চারটি মৌলিক ঋতুর অংশ নয়।

---

### Examples

My favorite season is winter.

আমার প্রিয় ঋতু শীত।

---

Summer is very hot.

গ্রীষ্ম অনেক গরম।

---

Spring is beautiful.

বসন্ত সুন্দর।

---

I like rainy days.

আমি বৃষ্টির দিন পছন্দ করি।

---

# 💬 70 Daily Speaking Sentences

## Weather

1. It's sunny today.
2. It's raining now.
3. It's cloudy outside.
4. It's very hot today.
5. It's cold this morning.
6. It's windy today.
7. The weather is nice.
8. The weather is changing.
9. It's getting warmer.
10. It's getting colder.

---

## Daily Conversation

11. How's the weather?
12. It's great.
13. It's terrible.
14. I like today's weather.
15. I don't like hot weather.
16. I love rainy days.
17. I enjoy cool mornings.
18. I always carry an umbrella.
19. Don't forget your jacket.
20. It's freezing outside.

---

## Seasons

21. My favorite season is winter.
22. I like spring.
23. Summer is too hot.
24. Autumn is beautiful.
25. Winter is cold.
26. It rains a lot during the rainy season.
27. Flowers bloom in spring.
28. Trees lose their leaves in autumn.
29. The days are longer in summer.
30. I wear warm clothes in winter.

---

## Everyday Use

31. Take an umbrella.
32. Wear a coat.
33. Wear a hat.
34. Stay hydrated.
35. Drink more water.
36. Be careful on the wet road.
37. The sky is clear.
38. The sun is shining.
39. I love fresh air.
40. It's a beautiful day.

---

## Feelings

41. I feel cold.
42. I feel hot.
43. I feel comfortable.
44. The weather makes me happy.
45. Rain helps me relax.
46. I enjoy walking in cool weather.
47. I don't like strong winds.
48. I love watching the rain.
49. The weather affects my mood.
50. Today feels refreshing.

---

## More Useful Sentences

51. It's going to rain.
52. The forecast says it will be sunny.
53. The weather changes quickly.
54. It's a perfect day for a walk.
55. Let's stay indoors.
56. Open the window.
57. Close the window.
58. Turn on the fan.
59. Turn on the air conditioner.
60. The room is too hot.
61. The room is too cold.
62. I need a sweater.
63. I enjoy winter mornings.
64. The air feels fresh.
65. It's a lovely evening.
66. The sun is setting.
67. The sky looks beautiful.
68. I love nature.
69. Let's go outside.
70. Have a wonderful day!

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Weather

**A:** How's the weather today?

**B:** It's sunny and warm.

**A:** That's nice!

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Rain

**A:** Is it raining outside?

**B:** Yes, it is.

**A:** Don't forget your umbrella.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Favorite Season

**A:** What's your favorite season?

**B:** My favorite season is winter.

**A:** Why?

**B:** Because I enjoy cool weather.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Summer

**A:** Do you like summer?

**B:** Not really.

**A:** Why not?

**B:** Because it's too hot.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Going Outside

**A:** Shall we go for a walk?

**B:** Sure! The weather is perfect.

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word     | Easy Pronunciation |
| -------- | ------------------ |
| Weather  | ওয়ে-দার           |
| Sunny    | সা-নি              |
| Rainy    | রেই-নি             |
| Cloudy   | ক্লাউ-ডি           |
| Windy    | উইন-ডি             |
| Autumn   | অ-টাম              |
| Winter   | উইন-টার            |
| Forecast | ফোর-কাস্ট          |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips

শুধু **"It's hot."** বলার পরিবর্তে আরও স্বাভাবিকভাবে বলো।

❌ It's hot.

✅ It's really hot today.

✅ It's getting hotter.

✅ I think it's too hot to go outside.

---

# 🗣️ Speaking Challenge

নিচের বাক্যগুলো **৫ বার** জোরে জোরে বলো।

1. How's the weather today?
2. It's sunny and warm.
3. I love rainy days.
4. My favorite season is winter.
5. It's getting colder.
6. Don't forget your umbrella.
7. The weather is beautiful today.
8. I enjoy walking in cool weather.
9. The sky looks beautiful.
10. Have a wonderful day!

---

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. "আজ আবহাওয়া কেমন?"

A. How's the weather today?

B. What weather today?

C. How weather is?

---

### 2. "আজ বৃষ্টি হচ্ছে।"

A. It's raining today.

B. It raining today.

C. It's rain today.

---

### 3. "আমার প্রিয় ঋতু শীত।"

A. My favorite season is winter.

B. My favorite winter season.

C. I favorite season winter.

---

### 4. "একটি ছাতা নিয়ে যাও।"

A. Take an umbrella.

B. Take umbrella.

C. Bring a umbrella.

---

### 5. "আজ আকাশ মেঘলা।"

A. It's cloudy today.

B. It cloudy today.

C. Sky cloudy.

---

# 🌟 Daily Mission

আজ অন্তত **৫ মিনিট** ইংরেজিতে আবহাওয়া নিয়ে কথা বলো।

উদাহরণ:

> Today is sunny. It's a little warm. I like this weather because it's comfortable. My favorite season is winter because I enjoy cool mornings.

| -----: | --------- |
|      1 | One       |
|      2 | Two       |

|      9 | Nine      |
|     10 | Ten       |
|     11 | Eleven    |
|     12 | Twelve    |
|     13 | Thirteen  |
|     14 | Fourteen  |
|     15 | Fifteen   |
|     16 | Sixteen   |
|     17 | Seventeen |
|     18 | Eighteen  |
|     19 | Nineteen  |
|     20 | Twenty    |

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Bigger Numbers

| Number    | English              |
| --------- | -------------------- |
| 30        | Thirty               |
| 40        | Forty                |
| 50        | Fifty                |
| 60        | Sixty                |
| 70        | Seventy              |
| 80        | Eighty               |
| 90        | Ninety               |
| 100       | One hundred          |
| 1,000     | One thousand         |
| 10,000    | Ten thousand         |
| 100,000   | One hundred thousand |
| 1,000,000 | One million          |

### Examples

* I have two hundred taka.
* The laptop costs fifty thousand taka.
* There are one hundred students in the hall.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Talking About Money

### Useful Questions

**How much is this?**

= এটার দাম কত?

---

**How much does it cost?**

= এটার দাম কত?

---

**Can I pay by card?**

= আমি কি কার্ড দিয়ে পেমেন্ট করতে পারি?

---

**Do you accept cash?**

= আপনারা কি নগদ টাকা নেন?

---

### Useful Answers

* It's 500 taka.
* It costs 2,000 taka.
* That's too expensive.
* That's affordable.
* I'll take it.
* I'll think about it.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: Shopping Vocabulary

| --------- | ---------- |

| Customer  | ক্রেতা     |
| Cashier   | ক্যাশিয়ার |
| Price     | দাম        |
| Discount  | ছাড়       |
| Expensive | দামি       |
| Cheap     | সস্তা      |
| Receipt   | রসিদ       |
| Cash      | নগদ টাকা   |
| Card      | কার্ড      |
| Wallet    | মানিব্যাগ  |
| Change    | ফেরত টাকা  |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 5: Shopping Expressions

* I'm just looking.
* Can I help you?
* I'd like to buy this.
* Do you have a different size?
* Do you have this in black?
* Can you give me a discount?
* I'll pay in cash.
* I'll pay by card.
* Can I get a receipt?
* Thank you for your help.

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Buying a T-shirt

**Customer:** Excuse me, how much is this T-shirt?

**Shopkeeper:** It's 800 taka.

**Customer:** Do you have a larger size?

**Shopkeeper:** Yes, we do.

**Customer:** Great! I'll take it.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Asking for a Discount

**Customer:** Can you give me a discount?

**Shopkeeper:** I can give you 10% off.

**Customer:** Thank you!

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Payment

**Cashier:** How would you like to pay?

**Customer:** I'll pay by card.

**Cashier:** Here is your receipt.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Looking Around

**Shopkeeper:** Can I help you?

**Customer:** I'm just looking, thank you.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Returning an Item

**Customer:** I'd like to return this item.

**Cashier:** Do you have the receipt?

**Customer:** Yes, here it is.

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word       | Easy Pronunciation |
| ---------- | ------------------ |
| Price      | প্রাইস             |
| Discount   | ডিস-কাউন্ট         |
| Receipt    | রি-সিট *(p নীরব)*  |
| Wallet     | ওয়াল-লেট          |
| Customer   | কাস-টা-মার         |
| Cashier    | ক্যা-শিয়ার        |
| Expensive  | এক্স-পেন-সিভ       |
| Affordable | অ্যা-ফোর্ড-অ্যাবল  |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips

দাম জিজ্ঞাসা করার সময় শুধু **"Price?"** বলো না।

❌ Price?

✅ How much is this?

✅ How much does it cost?

---

পেমেন্টের সময়:

❌ Card.

✅ I'll pay by card.

---

# ✅ Mini Quiz

C. Pay by card I.

B. You give discount?

C. Discount give me?

### 5. "এটা খুব দামি।"

B. It's much expensive.

C. It expensive too.

# 🌟 Daily Mission

আজ বাড়িতে ৫ মিনিটের একটি **Shopping Role-play** করো।

নিজেই Customer এবং Shopkeeper-এর ভূমিকা পালন করো।

**Customer:**

* How much is this?
* Do you have a different size?
* Can you give me a discount?

**Shopkeeper:**

* It's 800 taka.
* Yes, we do.
* Here's your receipt.

এই অনুশীলন তোমার বাস্তব জীবনের ইংরেজি কথোপকথনের আত্মবিশ্বাস অনেক বাড়িয়ে দেবে।

# ✅ Day 9: Restaurant English – Ordering Food & Dining Conversation

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Restaurant Vocabulary

| English      | বাংলা         |
| ------------ | ------------- |
| Restaurant   | রেস্টুরেন্ট   |
| Menu         | মেনু          |
| Waiter       | ওয়েটার       |
| Waitress     | ওয়েট্রেস     |
| Customer     | ক্রেতা        |
| Table        | টেবিল         |
| Chair        | চেয়ার        |
| Order        | অর্ডার        |
| Dish         | খাবারের পদ    |
| Meal         | খাবার         |
| Breakfast    | নাস্তা        |
| Lunch        | দুপুরের খাবার |
| Dinner       | রাতের খাবার   |
| Dessert      | মিষ্টান্ন     |
| Drink        | পানীয়        |
| Bill / Check | বিল           |
| Tip          | বকশিশ         |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Useful Restaurant Expressions

### Entering the Restaurant

* Hello!
* Good evening.
* A table for one, please.
* A table for two, please.
* Is there any table available?

---

### Asking for the Menu

* May I have the menu, please?
* Could I see the menu?
* What's today's special?

---

### Ordering Food

* I'd like to order, please.
* I'd like a chicken burger.
* I'll have fried rice.
* I'd like a glass of water.
* Can I have some juice?

---

### Asking About Food

* What's in this dish?
* Is it spicy?
* Is it vegetarian?
* Is it fresh?
* What do you recommend?

---

### During the Meal

* The food is delicious.
* This tastes great.
* Could I have some more water?
* Excuse me!

---

### Paying the Bill

* Could I have the bill, please?
* Can I pay by card?
* I'll pay in cash.
* Keep the change.
* Thank you!

---

# 💬 70 Daily Speaking Sentences

## At the Restaurant

1. I'd like a table for two.
2. May I have the menu?
3. What's today's special?
4. I'd like to order.
5. I'll have fried rice.
6. I'd like grilled chicken.
7. I'll take a salad.
8. I'd like a cup of tea.
9. Can I have some water?
10. Thank you.

---

## Asking Questions

11. Is this dish spicy?
12. Is this vegetarian?
13. What's in this soup?
14. Do you have seafood?
15. Which dish do you recommend?
16. Is breakfast available now?
17. Do you serve coffee?
18. Is there any dessert?
19. Can I change my order?
20. How long will it take?

---

## During the Meal

21. The food is delicious.
22. It tastes amazing.
23. This is very spicy.
24. I love this dish.
25. The soup is hot.
26. The rice is fresh.
27. Could I have another spoon?
28. May I have a fork?
29. Could I get a knife?
30. Everything is perfect.

---

## Paying

31. Could I have the bill?
32. How much is it?
33. Can I pay by card?
34. I'll pay in cash.
35. Keep the change.
36. Here's my card.
37. Thank you for the service.
38. Have a nice day.
39. See you again.
40. Goodbye.

---

## Food Preferences

41. I like spicy food.
42. I don't eat beef.
43. I prefer chicken.
44. I love fish.
45. I drink coffee every morning.
46. I enjoy fresh juice.
47. Water is enough for me.
48. I don't like cold drinks.
49. I usually eat healthy food.
50. I love homemade food.

---

## Everyday Restaurant English

51. I'm hungry.
52. I'm thirsty.
53. Let's have lunch.
54. Let's eat together.
55. What would you like to eat?
56. I'd like pizza.
57. I'm full.
58. The service was excellent.
59. The restaurant is clean.
60. I enjoyed the meal.
61. The food arrived quickly.
62. The waiter was polite.
63. This place is popular.
64. I want to come here again.
65. The food was worth the price.
66. I highly recommend this restaurant.
67. The atmosphere is relaxing.
68. We had a great dinner.
69. Thank you for everything.
70. See you next time!

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Ordering Food

**Waiter:** Good evening. Welcome!

**Customer:** Good evening. A table for two, please.

**Waiter:** This way, please.

**Customer:** Thank you.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Choosing Food

**Waiter:** Are you ready to order?

**Customer:** Yes. I'll have fried rice and grilled chicken.

**Waiter:** Anything to drink?

**Customer:** A glass of orange juice, please.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Asking About Food

**Customer:** Is this dish spicy?

**Waiter:** Yes, it's a little spicy.

**Customer:** That's fine. I'll take it.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Paying the Bill

**Customer:** Could I have the bill, please?

**Waiter:** Certainly.

**Customer:** Can I pay by card?

**Waiter:** Yes, of course.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Giving Feedback

**Waiter:** How was your meal?

**Customer:** It was delicious. Thank you!

**Waiter:** We're glad you enjoyed it.

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word       | Easy Pronunciation |
| ---------- | ------------------ |
| Restaurant | রেস-টা-রান্ট       |
| Menu       | মেন-ইউ             |
| Waiter     | ওয়ে-টার           |
| Dessert    | ডি-জার্ট           |
| Delicious  | ডি-লিশ-আস          |
| Receipt    | রি-সিট *(p নীরব)*  |
| Service    | সার-ভিস            |
| Recommend  | রে-কো-মেন্ড        |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips

রেস্টুরেন্টে ভদ্রভাবে কথা বলার জন্য **please**, **could**, **may** ব্যবহার করো।

❌ Give me water.

✅ Could I have some water, please?

---

❌ Bill.

✅ Could I have the bill, please?

---

❌ Chicken.

✅ I'd like grilled chicken, please.

---

# 🗣️ Speaking Challenge

নিচের বাক্যগুলো **৫ বার** জোরে জোরে বলো।

1. A table for two, please.
2. May I have the menu?
3. I'd like to order.
4. I'll have fried rice and chicken.
5. Could I have some water, please?
6. Is this dish spicy?
7. The food is delicious.
8. Could I have the bill, please?
9. Can I pay by card?
10. Thank you. Have a nice day!

---

# 📝 Homework

## Part 1 – Write

**"My Favorite Restaurant"** বিষয়ে **১০–১২টি ইংরেজি বাক্য** লিখো।

এগুলো অন্তর্ভুক্ত করো:

* Restaurant name (বাস্তব বা কাল্পনিক)
* Favorite food
* Why you like it
* Service
* Price
* Atmosphere

* Asking for a table
* Ordering food
* Asking for water

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. "মেনুটা কি দেখতে পারি?"

A. May I have the menu, please?

B. Give menu.

C. Menu show.

---

### 2. "আমি ফ্রাইড রাইস অর্ডার করতে চাই।"

A. I'd like to order fried rice.

B. I order fried rice want.

C. Fried rice I like order.

---

### 3. "এই খাবারটি কি ঝাল?"

A. Is this dish spicy?

B. This dish spicy?

C. Dish is spicy it?

---

### 4. "বিলটা দিতে পারবেন?"

A. Could I have the bill, please?

B. Give bill.

C. Bill please give.

---

### 5. "খাবারটা খুব সুস্বাদু।"

A. The food is delicious.

B. Food delicious.

C. The food delicious is.

# 🌟 Daily Mission

আজ বাড়িতে **Restaurant Role-play** করো।

**তুমি Customer এবং Waiter—দুই ভূমিকাতেই কথা বলো।**

**Customer:**

* Good evening.
* A table for one, please.
* May I have the menu?
* I'd like fried rice and chicken.
* Could I have the bill, please?

**Waiter:**

* Welcome!
* Here's the menu.
* Anything to drink?
* Here's your bill.
* Thank you. Have a nice day!

🎯 **আজকের লক্ষ্য:** অন্তত **৫ মিনিট** শুধুই ইংরেজিতে এই কথোপকথন অনুশীলন করা।

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Airport English

### Common Sentences

* Where is the check-in counter?
* Here is my passport.
* Here is my ticket.
* Can I have a window seat?
* Where is Gate 5?
* What time does the flight depart?
* Is the flight on time?
* Where can I collect my baggage?
* Thank you.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Bus & Train English

### Buying a Ticket

* I'd like one ticket to Dhaka.
* How much is the ticket?
* What time does the bus leave?
* Which platform is it?
* Is this seat available?
* When will we arrive?

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: Hotel English

### Check-in

* I have a reservation.
* I'd like to check in.
* Here is my ID.
* Is breakfast included?
* What time is check-out?
* Could I have the room key?

---

### Check-out

* I'd like to check out.
* Could I have the bill?
* Thank you for your service.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 5: Asking for Directions

### Useful Questions

* Excuse me, where is the bus station?
* How can I get to the airport?
* Which way is the hotel?
* Is it far from here?
* Can you show me on the map?

### Useful Answers

* Go straight.
* Turn left.
* Turn right.
* It's next to the bank.
* It's across from the hospital.
* It's about ten minutes away.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – At the Airport

**Staff:** Good morning. May I see your passport?

**Passenger:** Sure. Here is my passport and boarding pass.

**Staff:** Thank you. Your gate is B12.

**Passenger:** Thank you very much.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Buying a Bus Ticket

**Customer:** I'd like one ticket to Dhaka, please.

**Clerk:** That will be 800 taka.

**Customer:** Here you are.

**Clerk:** Thank you.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Hotel Check-in

**Receptionist:** Welcome! Do you have a reservation?

**Guest:** Yes, I do.

**Receptionist:** May I see your ID?

**Guest:** Certainly.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Asking for Directions

**Tourist:** Excuse me, where is the railway station?

**Local:** Go straight, then turn left.

**Tourist:** Thank you.

**Local:** You're welcome.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Taking a Taxi

**Passenger:** Please take me to the airport.

**Driver:** Sure. It will take about 30 minutes.

**Passenger:** Thank you.

---

| Reservation  | রে-জার-ভে-শন       |
| Boarding     | বোর্ড-ইং           |
| Platform     | প্ল্যাট-ফর্ম       |
| Journey      | জার-নি             |
| Direction    | ডাই-রেক-শন         |
| Receptionist | রি-সেপ-শ-নিস্ট     |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips

ভ্রমণের সময় **Could you...**, **Can you...**, **May I...** ব্যবহার করলে কথা আরও ভদ্র শোনায়।

❌ Where is the airport?

✅ Excuse me, where is the airport?

---

❌ Give me the bill.

✅ Could I have the bill, please?

---

❌ Taxi!

✅ Could you call a taxi, please?

---

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. "আমার একটি বুকিং আছে।"

A. I have a reservation.

B. I have reservation.

C. I reservation have.

---

### 2. "চেক-ইন কাউন্টার কোথায়?"

B. Check-in where?

C. Where check-in counter?

---

### 3. "আমি ঢাকার একটি টিকিট চাই।"

A. I'd like one ticket to Dhaka.

B. I like ticket Dhaka.

C. Give ticket Dhaka.

---

### 4. "সোজা যান, তারপর ডানে ঘুরুন।"

A. Go straight, then turn right.

B. Straight go right.

C. Go right then straight.

---

### 5. "আপনার যাত্রা শুভ হোক।"

A. Have a safe journey.

B. Journey safe.

C. Safe travel you.

# ✅ Day 11: Health & Doctor English – Symptoms, Medicine & Pharmacy

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 💊 Pharmacy থেকে ওষুধ কেনা

* 📝 Homework

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Health Vocabulary

| English      | বাংলা            |
| ------------ | ---------------- |

| Patient      | রোগী             |
| Hospital     | হাসপাতাল         |

| Medicine     | ওষুধ             |

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Common Symptoms

| English     | বাংলা        |
| ----------- | ------------ |
| Fever       | জ্বর         |
| Cold        | সর্দি        |
| Cough       | কাশি         |
| Headache    | মাথাব্যথা    |
| Toothache   | দাঁতের ব্যথা |
| Stomachache | পেটব্যথা     |
| Sore throat | গলা ব্যথা    |
| Back pain   | পিঠে ব্যথা   |
| Dizziness   | মাথা ঘোরা    |
| Tired       | ক্লান্ত      |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Telling the Doctor About Your Problem

### Useful Sentences

* I have a fever.
* I have a headache.
* I have a cough.
* My throat hurts.
* I don't feel well.
* I've been sick for two days.
* I feel weak.
* I have a stomachache.
* I have a runny nose.
* I can't sleep well.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: Doctor's Questions

* What's the problem?
* How long have you had this?
* Do you have a fever?
* Does it hurt?
* Are you taking any medicine?
* Are you allergic to anything?

---

# 🎯 Lesson 5: Doctor's Advice

* Take this medicine twice a day.
* Drink plenty of water.
* Get some rest.
* Eat healthy food.
* Avoid oily food.
* Come back next week.
* You should sleep more.
* You need a blood test.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 6: At the Pharmacy

### Useful Sentences

* I need some medicine.
* Do I need a prescription?
* How often should I take this?
* Are there any side effects?
* Thank you.

---

# 💬 80 Daily Speaking Sentences

## Feeling Sick

1. I don't feel well.
2. I have a fever.
3. I have a cold.
4. I have a cough.
5. I have a headache.
6. My back hurts.
7. My stomach hurts.
8. I feel tired.
9. I feel weak.
10. I need a doctor.

---

## Visiting the Doctor

11. I'd like to see a doctor.
12. I have an appointment.
13. What's the problem?
14. I have a sore throat.
15. Since when have you felt sick?
16. Since yesterday.
17. Please take a deep breath.
18. Open your mouth, please.
19. Your temperature is normal.
20. Your blood pressure is fine.

---

## Medicine

21. Take this medicine after meals.
22. Take it twice a day.
23. Drink plenty of water.
24. Get enough sleep.
25. Don't skip your medicine.
26. Finish the full course.
27. This medicine will help.
28. Follow the doctor's advice.
29. Keep the medicine away from children.
30. Store it in a cool place.

---

## Pharmacy

31. I need pain medicine.
32. Do you have cough syrup?
33. Is this medicine available?
34. How much does it cost?
35. Do I need a prescription?
36. Can you explain how to take it?
37. Are there any side effects?
38. Thank you for your help.
39. I'll take it.
40. Have a nice day.

---

## Healthy Habits

41. I exercise every day.
42. I eat healthy food.
43. I drink enough water.
44. I sleep eight hours.
45. I avoid junk food.
46. I walk every morning.
47. I don't smoke.
48. I don't drink alcohol.
49. Health is wealth.
50. Prevention is better than cure.

---

## Emergency

51. Call an ambulance!
52. I need help.
53. It's an emergency.
54. Please call a doctor.
55. Stay calm.
56. Help is on the way.
57. Can you hear me?
58. Are you okay?
59. Don't move.
60. We'll take care of you.

---

## More Useful Sentences

61. I feel much better today.
62. Thank you, doctor.
63. The medicine is working.
64. I still have pain.
65. I need another appointment.
66. My symptoms have improved.
67. I'm recovering well.
68. I hope you get well soon.
69. Take care of yourself.
70. Stay healthy.
71. I have an allergy.
72. I feel dizzy.
73. My nose is blocked.
74. I can't stop coughing.
75. I have a toothache.
76. I need to visit a dentist.
77. My eyes hurt.
78. I feel stressed.
79. I need some rest.
80. Everything will be okay.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – At the Doctor's Clinic

**Doctor:** What's the problem?

**Patient:** I have a fever and a headache.

**Doctor:** Since when?

**Patient:** Since yesterday.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Medical Advice

**Doctor:** Drink plenty of water and take this medicine twice a day.

**Patient:** Thank you, doctor.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – At the Pharmacy

**Customer:** I need cough syrup.

**Pharmacist:** Here you are.

**Customer:** How often should I take it?

**Pharmacist:** Three times a day after meals.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Emergency

**Person A:** Are you okay?

**Person B:** I feel dizzy.

**Person A:** Sit down. I'll call for help.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Recovery

**Friend:** How are you feeling now?

**You:** I'm feeling much better. Thanks for asking.

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word         | Easy Pronunciation |
| ------------ | ------------------ |
| Fever        | ফি-ভার             |
| Headache     | হেড-এক             |
| Medicine     | মেডি-সিন           |
| Prescription | প্রি-স্ক্রিপ-শন    |
| Appointment  | আ-পয়েন্ট-মেন্ট    |
| Allergy      | অ্যালার-জি         |
| Pharmacy     | ফার-মা-সি          |
| Ambulance    | অ্যাম-বিউ-ল্যান্স  |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips

শরীর খারাপ লাগলে শুধু **"I'm sick."** বলেই থেমে যেও না।

❌ I'm sick.

✅ I have a fever and a sore throat.

✅ I don't feel well today.

---

ডাক্তারের কাছে:

❌ Medicine.

✅ Could you explain how I should take this medicine?

---

# 🗣️ Speaking Challenge

নিচের বাক্যগুলো **৫ বার** বলো।

1. I don't feel well.
2. I have a headache.
3. I'd like to see a doctor.
4. I need some medicine.
5. Take this medicine twice a day.
6. Drink plenty of water.
7. I feel much better now.
8. Thank you, doctor.
9. Stay healthy.
10. Get well soon.

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. "আমার জ্বর হয়েছে।"

A. I have a fever.

B. I am fever.

C. I have fevered.

---

### 2. "আমি একজন ডাক্তারকে দেখতে চাই।"

A. I'd like to see a doctor.

B. I want doctor see.

C. I see doctor like.

---

### 3. "প্রতিদিন দুইবার ওষুধ খান।"

A. Take this medicine twice a day.

B. Take medicine two day.

C. Medicine twice take.

---

### 4. "আমার মাথাব্যথা করছে।"

A. I have a headache.

B. My head pain.

C. I headache.

---

### 5. "দয়া করে প্রচুর পানি পান করুন।"

A. Drink plenty of water.

B. Drink many water.

C. Please drink much waters.

* Since yesterday.

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Office Vocabulary

| English      | বাংলা              |
| ------------ | ------------------ |
| Office       | অফিস               |
| Company      | কোম্পানি           |
| Employee     | কর্মচারী           |
| Employer     | নিয়োগকর্তা        |
| Manager      | ম্যানেজার          |
| Team         | টিম                |
| Colleague    | সহকর্মী            |
| Meeting      | মিটিং              |
| Project      | প্রজেক্ট           |
| Deadline     | নির্ধারিত সময়সীমা |
| Task         | কাজ                |
| Client       | ক্লায়েন্ট         |
| Report       | রিপোর্ট            |
| Presentation | উপস্থাপনা          |
| Interview    | সাক্ষাৎকার         |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Self-Introduction in an Interview

### Example

> Good morning.

> My name is Md. Atiar Rahman.

> I am a Full Stack Developer with experience in Python, Django, Django REST Framework, JavaScript, and React.

> I enjoy solving real-world problems by building web applications.

> I am a quick learner, a team player, and always willing to improve my skills.

> Thank you for giving me this opportunity.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Common Interview Questions

### 1. Tell me about yourself.

**Answer:**

My name is Md. Atiar Rahman. I am passionate about web development. I enjoy building modern web applications using Python, Django, Django REST Framework, JavaScript, and React. I am always eager to learn new technologies and improve my skills.

---

### 2. Why do you want to work here?

I want to work here because your company values innovation and learning. I believe I can grow professionally while contributing to your team.

---

### 3. What are your strengths?

* I am hardworking.
* I learn quickly.
* I enjoy solving problems.
* I work well in a team.
* I am responsible.

---

### 4. What is your weakness?

I sometimes spend too much time perfecting my work, but I am learning to manage my time more effectively.

---

### 5. Where do you see yourself in five years?

I see myself as a skilled software engineer leading successful projects and continuously learning new technologies.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: Office Communication

### Asking for Help

* Could you help me, please?
* Can you explain this task?
* Could you review my code?
* I need your advice.

---

### During Meetings

* Let's begin the meeting.
* What's the agenda?
* I agree.
* I disagree.
* That's a good idea.
* Could you explain that again?
* Let's discuss this later.
* I'll take notes.

---

### Talking About Work

* I'm working on a new project.
* I finished the task.
* I'm almost done.
* I need more time.
* The deadline is tomorrow.
* I'll send the report today.

---

# 💬 80 Daily Speaking Sentences

## Office

5. I need your help.
6. Could you explain this?
7. I'll send the email.

9. The deadline is tomorrow.

## Daily Office English

57. The project is going well.
58. Everything is under control.

## More Useful Sentences

61. I'll share the file.
62. Please review it.
63. Let's fix the issue.
64. We found the problem.
65. The solution works well.
66. The client is satisfied.
67. I'll prepare the presentation.
68. Thank you for your support.

70. Have a great weekend.
71. I completed the assignment.
72. We need more testing.
73. I'll deploy the application tomorrow.
74. The server is running well.
75. The website is live.
76. I fixed the bug.
77. Let's push the code.
78. Please review the pull request.
79. I'll update the documentation.
80. The feature is ready.

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Job Interview

**Interviewer:** Tell me about yourself.

**Candidate:** My name is Md. Atiar Rahman. I'm a Full Stack Developer. I enjoy building web applications with Python, Django, Django REST Framework, JavaScript, and React.

**Interviewer:** Why do you want to join our company?

**Candidate:** Because I want to learn, grow, and contribute to meaningful projects.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Office Meeting

**Manager:** Good morning, everyone.

**Employee:** Good morning.

**Manager:** Let's begin today's meeting.

**Employee:** Sure.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Asking for Help

**Employee:** Could you review my code?

**Colleague:** Of course.

**Employee:** Thank you.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Teamwork

**Manager:** Can you finish this today?

**Employee:** Yes, I'll complete it before the deadline.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Client Meeting

**Client:** Is the project ready?

**Developer:** Yes. The main features are complete, and we're doing the final testing.

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word           | Easy Pronunciation  |
| -------------- | ------------------- |
| Employee       | এম-প্লয়-ই          |
| Colleague      | কল-লিগ              |
| Interview      | ইন-টার-ভিউ          |
| Deadline       | ডেড-লাইন            |
| Presentation   | প্রে-জেন-টেই-শন     |
| Professional   | প্রো-ফে-শন-আল       |
| Responsibility | রি-স্পন-সি-বি-লি-টি |
| Feedback       | ফিড-ব্যাক           |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips

অফিসে ভদ্র ও পেশাদার ভাষা ব্যবহার করো।

❌ Send the file.

✅ Could you please send the file?

---

❌ I don't know.

✅ I'm not sure, but I'll check and let you know.

---

❌ Wait.

✅ Could you please wait for a moment?

---

নিচের বাক্যগুলো **৫ বার** বলো।

3. I'm working on a new project.

5. I'll send the report today.
6. Let's begin the meeting.
7. Thank you for your feedback.
8. The project is going well.
9. I appreciate your support.
10. Have a productive day.

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. "নিজের সম্পর্কে বলুন।"

A. Tell me about yourself.

B. Say yourself.

C. Speak yourself.

---

### 2. "আমি একটি নতুন প্রজেক্টে কাজ করছি।"

A. I'm working on a new project.

B. I working new project.

C. I am work on project.

---

### 3. "আপনি কি আমার কোড রিভিউ করতে পারবেন?"

A. Could you review my code?

B. Review my code you?

C. You review code?

---

### 4. "আমি আজ রিপোর্ট পাঠাব।"

A. I'll send the report today.

B. I send report today.

C. Today report send.

---

### 5. "ডেডলাইন আগামীকাল।"

A. The deadline is tomorrow.

B. Deadline tomorrow.

C. Tomorrow deadline is.

### 👔 Interview

* What are your strengths?
* Why do you want to work here?

### 💼 Office

* I'm working on a new project.
* Could you review my code?
* I'll finish the task today.

### 🤝 Meeting

* Let's begin the meeting.
* I agree with your idea.
* Thank you for your feedback.

# ✅ Day 13: Telephone & Video Call English – Online Meetings & Customer Support

* 🎧 Customer Support-এর সাথে কথা বলা

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Telephone Vocabulary

| English       | বাংলা               |
| ------------- | ------------------- |
| Phone Call    | ফোন কল              |
| Mobile Phone  | মোবাইল ফোন          |
| Telephone     | টেলিফোন             |
| Call          | কল                  |
| Missed Call   | মিসড কল             |
| Voice Message | ভয়েস মেসেজ         |
| Contact       | যোগাযোগ             |
| Signal        | নেটওয়ার্ক সিগন্যাল |
| Battery       | ব্যাটারি            |
| Charger       | চার্জার             |
| Speaker       | স্পিকার             |
| Microphone    | মাইক্রোফোন          |
| Headphones    | হেডফোন              |
| Network       | নেটওয়ার্ক          |
| Call Back     | আবার কল করা         |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Starting a Phone Call

### Common Expressions

* Hello!
* Hi, this is Atiar speaking.
* May I speak to Mr. Rahman?
* Is this the right number?
* Who's calling, please?
* Can you hear me?
* Am I speaking with the manager?

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: During the Phone Call

### Useful Sentences

* The line is breaking up.
* I can't hear you clearly.
* Could you speak more slowly?
* Could you repeat that, please?
* Please hold for a moment.
* I'll call you back.
* One moment, please.
* Sorry, I missed your call.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: Video Call & Online Meeting

### Useful Expressions

* Can you hear me?
* Can you see my screen?
* I'll share my screen.
* Your microphone is muted.
* Please turn on your camera.
* The internet connection is slow.
* Let's start the meeting.
* Any questions?

---

# 🎯 Lesson 5: Customer Support English

### Asking for Help

* I need some help.
* I'm having a problem with my account.
* I forgot my password.
* I can't log in.
* My payment failed.
* Could you help me?
* Thank you for your support.

---

# 💬 80 Daily Speaking Sentences

## Telephone

1. Hello.
2. Hi, this is Atiar speaking.
3. May I speak to John?
4. Who's calling?
5. This is my friend.
6. Is this the right number?
7. Sorry, wrong number.
8. I'll call you later.
9. Please call me back.
10. Thank you for calling.

---

## During the Call

11. Can you hear me?
12. I can't hear you.
13. Your voice is unclear.
14. The signal is weak.
15. The call was disconnected.
16. Could you repeat that?
17. Please speak slowly.
18. One moment, please.
19. Please hold.
20. I'm listening.

---

## Video Meeting

21. Good morning, everyone.
22. Can you see my screen?
23. I'll share my screen.
24. Your microphone is muted.
25. Please turn on your camera.
26. The audio is clear.
27. The video is freezing.
28. The internet is slow.
29. Let's begin the meeting.
30. Thank you for joining.

---

## Customer Support

31. I need your help.
32. I forgot my password.
33. I can't log in.
34. My account is locked.
35. My payment failed.
36. Can you check my account?
37. The problem is solved.
38. Thank you for your support.
39. I appreciate your help.
40. Have a great day.

---

## Office Calls

41. Are you available now?
42. I'll call after lunch.
43. Let's discuss it tomorrow.
44. I'll send the details by email.
45. Did you receive my message?
46. Please confirm the meeting.
47. I'll join in five minutes.
48. I'm in another meeting.
49. I'll get back to you soon.
50. Thanks for your patience.

---

## Daily Phone English

51. My phone battery is low.
52. I need to charge my phone.
53. My phone is on silent mode.
54. I missed your message.
55. Please send me the location.
56. I'll text you.
57. Check your inbox.
58. I received your email.
59. I'll reply soon.
60. Let's stay in touch.

---

## More Useful Sentences

61. The connection is unstable.
62. Please reconnect.
63. Can you hear me now?
64. I think we lost the connection.
65. I'll restart my internet.
66. Sorry for the interruption.
67. Everything is working now.
68. Thank you for waiting.
69. See you in the next meeting.
70. Goodbye.
71. Can you email me the file?
72. I'll send the meeting link.
73. Please join on time.
74. The meeting starts at 10 a.m.
75. Let's end the meeting here.
76. Have a productive day.
77. Talk to you later.
78. Take care.
79. Have a nice evening.
80. Bye for now!

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Phone Call

**A:** Hello! This is Atiar speaking.

**B:** Hi! Can you talk now?

**A:** Yes, I can.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Poor Connection

**A:** Can you hear me?

**B:** Not clearly. The connection is weak.

**A:** I'll call you back.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Online Meeting

**Manager:** Good morning, everyone.

**Employee:** Good morning.

**Manager:** Can everyone see my screen?

**Employee:** Yes, we can.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Customer Support

**Customer:** I forgot my password.

**Support:** No problem. I'll help you reset it.

**Customer:** Thank you.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Scheduling a Call

**A:** Are you free this afternoon?

**B:** Yes. Let's talk at 3 p.m.

**A:** Sounds good!

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word       | Easy Pronunciation |
| ---------- | ------------------ |
| Microphone | মাই-ক্রো-ফোন       |
| Speaker    | স্পি-কার           |
| Connection | কান-নেক-শন         |
| Password   | পাস-ওয়ার্ড        |
| Account    | অ্যা-কাউন্ট        |
| Message    | মেস-এজ             |
| Meeting    | মি-টিং             |
| Support    | সা-পোর্ট           |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips

ফোনে ভদ্রভাবে কথা বলো।

❌ Hello, who are you?

✅ Hello, may I know who's calling, please?

---

ভিডিও মিটিংয়ে:

❌ I can't hear.

✅ I can't hear you clearly.

---

Customer Support-এ:

❌ My account problem.

✅ I'm having a problem with my account.

---

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. "আপনি কি আমাকে শুনতে পাচ্ছেন?"

A. Can you hear me?

B. Hear me you?

C. You hear me?

---

### 2. "আমি আপনাকে পরে কল করব।"

A. I'll call you back later.

B. I call you later.

C. Call later I.

---

### 3. "দয়া করে একটু অপেক্ষা করুন।"

A. Please hold for a moment.

B. Wait please moment.

C. Hold moment.

---

### 4. "আমি আমার পাসওয়ার্ড ভুলে গেছি।"

A. I forgot my password.

B. I forget password.

C. My password forgot.

---

### 5. "আমি আমার স্ক্রিন শেয়ার করব।"

A. I'll share my screen.

B. I share screen.

C. My screen share.

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Family Vocabulary

| English     | বাংলা                    |
| ----------- | ------------------------ |
| Family      | পরিবার                   |
| Father      | বাবা                     |
| Mother      | মা                       |
| Parents     | বাবা-মা                  |
| Brother     | ভাই                      |
| Sister      | বোন                      |
| Grandfather | দাদা/নানা                |
| Grandmother | দাদি/নানি                |
| Uncle       | চাচা/মামা                |
| Aunt        | ফুফু/খালা                |
| Cousin      | চাচাতো/মামাতো ভাই বা বোন |
| Son         | ছেলে                     |
| Daughter    | মেয়ে                    |
| Husband     | স্বামী                   |
| Wife        | স্ত্রী                   |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Talking About Your Family

### Examples

**There are five people in my family.**

আমার পরিবারে পাঁচজন সদস্য আছে।

---

**I live with my parents.**

আমি আমার বাবা-মায়ের সাথে থাকি।

---

**My father is a businessman.**

আমার বাবা একজন ব্যবসায়ী।

---

**My mother is a homemaker.**

আমার মা একজন গৃহিণী।

---

**I have one brother and one sister.**

আমার এক ভাই এবং এক বোন আছে।

---

| Window      | জানালা   |
| Floor       | মেঝে     |

| ------------------ | ------------------------- |

| Mop the floor      | মেঝে মোছা                 |
| Cook               | রান্না করা                |
| Do the laundry     | কাপড় ধোয়া               |
| Make the bed       | বিছানা গুছানো             |
| Take out the trash | ময়লা ফেলা                |
| Water the plants   | গাছে পানি দেওয়া          |
| Dust the furniture | আসবাবের ধুলো পরিষ্কার করা |

# 💬 80 Daily Speaking Sentences

## Family

2. My family is very supportive.
3. I live with my parents.

5. My mother is a homemaker.
6. I have one brother.
7. I have one sister.

10. Family is important to me.

20. It's time to sleep.

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Talking About Family

**A:** How many people are there in your family?

**B:** There are five people in my family.

**A:** Who do you live with?

**B:** I live with my parents and my younger brother.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – At Home

**Mother:** Could you help me clean the house?

**You:** Sure, Mom. I'll sweep the floor first.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Dinner Time

**Father:** Dinner is ready.

**You:** Great! Let's eat together.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Household Chores

**Brother:** Can you wash the dishes?

**You:** Yes, I'll do them after dinner.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Before Sleeping

**Mother:** Don't stay up too late.

**You:** Okay. Good night!

**Mother:** Good night. Sleep well.
