| ----------- | ------------------ |
| Family      | ফ্যা-মি-লি         |
| Parents     | পে-রেন্টস          |
| Kitchen     | কিচ-এন             |
| Laundry     | লন-ড্রি            |
| Comfortable | কাম্ফ-টার-বল       |
| Bedroom     | বেড-রুম            |
| Cousin      | কায-ন              |
| Furniture   | ফার-নি-চার         |

# 💡 Speaking Tips

পরিবার সম্পর্কে বলতে শুধু **"My family is good."** বলো না।

❌ My family is good.

✅ My family is very supportive.

✅ I enjoy spending time with my family.

---

বাড়ির কাজ সম্পর্কে:

❌ I clean.

✅ I'm cleaning my room.

✅ I usually help my mother with cooking.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Classroom English

### Teacher–Student Conversation

* May I come in, sir?
* May I go out, sir?
* I don’t understand.
* Please explain again.
* Can you repeat, please?
* I have a question.
* I finished my homework.
* I was absent yesterday.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Talking with Teachers

* Good morning, sir/madam.
* I have a doubt.
* Could you please help me?
* I didn’t understand this topic.
* Can you give an example?
* Thank you, sir.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: Exam English

* I have an exam tomorrow.
* I am preparing for my exam.
* The exam was difficult.
* I finished my paper.
* I need more time.
* I studied hard.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 5: Assignment & Study

* I have an assignment.
* I need to submit it tomorrow.
* I am working on it.
* I need reference materials.
* I will complete it soon.

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Classroom

**Teacher:** Open your books to page 10.

**Student:** Yes, sir.

**Teacher:** Do you understand?

**Student:** Not fully. Please explain again.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Asking Help

**Student:** Sir, I didn’t understand this topic.

**Teacher:** I will explain it again with an example.

**Student:** Thank you, sir.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Exam Talk

**Friend 1:** Are you ready for the exam?

**Friend 2:** Not fully, I am still revising.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Assignment

**Student:** I need to submit my assignment tomorrow.

**Friend:** Let’s complete it together.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – After Class

**Teacher:** Class is over.

**Students:** Thank you, sir!

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word       | Easy Pronunciation |
| ---------- | ------------------ |
| Student    | স্টু-ডেন্ট         |
| Teacher    | টি-চার             |
| Assignment | অ্যা-সাইন-মেন্ট    |
| Exam       | ইগ-জাম             |
| Library    | লাই-ব্রে-রি        |
| Subject    | সাব-জেক্ট          |
| Lecture    | লেক-চার            |
| Attendance | অ্যা-টেন-ডেন্স     |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips

ক্লাসে ভদ্রভাবে কথা বলো:

❌ I don’t understand this.

✅ I didn’t understand this. Could you please explain again?

---

❌ Help me.

✅ Could you please help me with this topic?

---

# 🗣️ Speaking Challenge

নিচের বাক্যগুলো **৫ বার** বলো:

1. May I come in, sir?
2. I don’t understand.
3. Please explain again.
4. I have an exam tomorrow.
5. I am preparing for my exam.
6. I have an assignment.
7. Good morning, sir.
8. Thank you for your help.
9. I will study hard.
10. Education is important.

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. "আমি একজন ছাত্র।"

C. I am study.

---

### 2. "দয়া করে আবার বুঝিয়ে বলুন।"

B. Explain again you.

C. Again explain please.

---

### 3. "আমি পরীক্ষার জন্য প্রস্তুতি নিচ্ছি।"

B. I prepare exam.

C. I am prepare exam.

---

### 4. "আমি একটি প্রশ্ন আছে।"

A. I have a question.

B. I question have.

C. Question I have.

---

### 5. "ক্লাস শেষ।"

A. The class is over.

B. Class over is.

C. Over class.

# ✅ Day 16: Shopping & Market English – Buying, Bargaining & Supermarket Conversation

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🛍️ Market & Shop English শেখা
* 💰 Price, Bargaining & Buying
* 🏪 Supermarket Conversation
* 💬 80+ Daily Speaking Sentences
* 🎭 Real-life Market Dialogues
* 🔊 Pronunciation Tips
* 📝 Homework
* ✅ Quiz

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Shopping Vocabulary

| English             | বাংলা        |
| ------------------- | ------------ |
| Shop / Store        | দোকান        |
| Market              | বাজার        |
| Supermarket         | সুপারমার্কেট |
| Customer            | ক্রেতা       |
| Seller / Shopkeeper | দোকানদার     |
| Price               | দাম          |
| Cheap               | সস্তা        |
| Expensive           | দামি         |
| Discount            | ছাড়         |
| Bargain             | দরদাম করা    |
| Buy                 | কেনা         |
| Sell                | বিক্রি করা   |
| Cash                | নগদ টাকা     |
| Change              | খুচরা টাকা   |
| Bill                | বিল          |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Useful Shopping Expressions

### 🛍️ Buying

* I want to buy this.
* How much is this?
* What is the price?
* I’ll take it.
* Do you have this in another size?
* Do you have this in another color?

---

### 💰 Bargaining

* Can you give me a discount?
* It’s too expensive.
* Make it cheaper, please.
* What is your last price?
* I’ll buy if you reduce the price.

---

### 🧾 Paying

* Here is the money.
* Keep the change.
* Can I pay by card?
* Do you accept mobile payment?

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Supermarket English

* Where is the milk section?
* Do you have fresh vegetables?
* I need rice and oil.
* Where is the billing counter?
* Is this item on sale?

---

# 💬 80 Daily Speaking Sentences

## 🛍️ Buying

1. How much is this?
2. What is the price?
3. I want to buy this.
4. I’ll take it.
5. It looks nice.
6. Do you have another one?
7. Do you have a smaller size?
8. Do you have a bigger size?
9. I like this color.
10. It’s very good.

---

## 💰 Bargaining

11. It’s too expensive.
12. Can you reduce the price?
13. Give me a discount.
14. What is your last price?
15. I can pay less.
16. Please make it cheaper.
17. I will buy if you reduce price.
18. That’s still expensive.
19. I’ll check another shop.
20. Okay, I’ll take it.

---

## 🏪 Shop Conversation

21. I’m looking for a shirt.
22. I need a mobile charger.
23. Do you have this model?
24. Show me something better.
25. I’m just looking.
26. I will come back later.
27. Do you have a warranty?
28. Is it original?
29. I want a new one.
30. Where is the cashier?

---

## 🧾 Payment

31. Can I pay by card?
32. Here is the money.
33. Do you accept mobile banking?
34. Give me a receipt.
35. Keep the change.
36. I need a bill.
37. It’s paid.
38. Thank you.
39. That’s all.
40. Have a nice day.

---

## 🏪 Supermarket

41. Where is the rice section?
42. Where is the vegetable section?
43. I need cooking oil.
44. Do you have fresh fruits?
45. Where is the billing counter?
46. Is this on discount?
47. I need a shopping bag.
48. The price is high.
49. I found what I need.
50. I’m done shopping.

---

## 💬 More Useful Sentences

51. This is very cheap.
52. This is very expensive.
53. I want a refund.
54. Do you have stock?
55. I like this shop.
56. The quality is good.
57. Show me another one.
58. I don’t like this.
59. I’ll think about it.
60. I’m not sure.

---

## 🛒 Daily Life Shopping

61. I go to the market every day.
62. I buy vegetables.
63. I buy fruits.
64. I buy groceries.
65. I shop once a week.
66. I prefer online shopping.
67. The market is crowded.
68. The shop is closed.
69. The price is reasonable.
70. I always compare prices.

---

## 🧠 Extra Sentences

71. Do you have a cheaper option?
72. I need a receipt.
73. It’s out of stock.
74. I want to exchange this.
75. It doesn’t fit me.
76. I like this design.
77. I need help.
78. I will come tomorrow.
79. Please pack it.
80. Thank you for your service.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – At a Shop

**Customer:** How much is this shirt?

**Shopkeeper:** It is 800 taka.

**Customer:** Can you give me a discount?

**Shopkeeper:** Okay, 700 taka.

**Customer:** I’ll take it.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Supermarket

**Customer:** Where is the rice section?

**Staff:** It’s over there.

**Customer:** Thank you.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Bargaining

**Customer:** It’s too expensive.

**Seller:** What is your offer?

**Customer:** I can pay 500 taka.

**Seller:** Okay, deal.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Payment

**Customer:** Can I pay by card?

**Cashier:** Yes, you can.

**Customer:** Here is my card.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – General Shopping

**Friend:** What are you buying?

**You:** I’m buying groceries.

**Friend:** Let’s go together.

---

| ---------- | ------------------ |
| Price      | প্রাইস             |
| Cheap      | চিপ                |
| Expensive  | এক্স-পেন-সিভ       |
| Discount   | ডিস-কাউন্ট         |
| Bargain    | বার-গেন            |
| Receipt    | রি-সিট             |
| Customer   | কাস্ট-মার          |
| Shopkeeper | শপ-কীপার           |

✅ How much is this?

---

❌ Give discount.

✅ Can you give me a discount?

---

❌ I buy this.

✅ I’ll take it.

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. "এটার দাম কত?"

A. How much is this?

B. What price this?

C. This how much?

---

### 2. "আমি এটা কিনবো।"

A. I’ll take it.

B. I take it.

C. Take I it.

---

### 3. "আপনি কি ডিসকাউন্ট দিতে পারেন?"

A. Can you give me a discount?

B. Give discount you?

C. Discount give me?

---

### 4. "আমি কিছু কিনতে চাই।"

A. I want to buy something.

B. I buy want something.

C. Buy I something.

---

### 5. "ধন্যবাদ।"

A. Thank you.

B. Thanks you.

C. You thank.

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Restaurant Vocabulary

| English     | বাংলা        |
| ----------- | ------------ |
| Restaurant  | রেস্টুরেন্ট  |
| Menu        | মেনু         |

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Ordering Food

### 🍽️ Useful Sentences

* What do you recommend?

* I’m vegetarian.

* It tastes great.
* It’s very spicy.
* I like it.
* This is too salty.
* Can I get some water?

* Could you bring the bill?
* Is service included?
* Keep the change.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 5: Complaints

* My food is cold.
* This is not what I ordered.
* It’s too salty.
* Can you replace it, please?
* I’m not satisfied.

# 💬 80 Daily Speaking Sentences

## 🍽️ Restaurant Basics

2. Let’s go to a restaurant.

5. The menu looks good.
6. I’m ready to order.
7. What is popular here?
8. I’ll try this.
9. I’ll take the same.
10. That sounds good.

## 🍔 Ordering Food

12. I want a burger.
13. I want a pizza.
14. Can I get water?
15. Do you have vegetarian food?

18. I’ll have this.

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Ordering Food

**Customer:** I’d like to see the menu, please.
**Waiter:** Here you are.
**Customer:** I’ll have rice and chicken.
**Waiter:** Anything to drink?
**Customer:** A glass of water, please.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Complaining

**Customer:** This food is cold.
**Waiter:** I’m sorry. I’ll replace it.
**Customer:** Thank you.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Restaurant Bill

**Customer:** Can I have the bill?
**Waiter:** Sure, here it is.
**Customer:** Keep the change.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Group Dining

**You:** I want pizza.
**Friend:** Good choice!

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Recommendation

**Customer:** What do you recommend?
**Waiter:** Our special chicken curry.
**Customer:** I’ll try that.

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Restaurant Vocabulary

| English     | বাংলা        |
| ----------- | ------------ |
| Restaurant  | রেস্টুরেন্ট  |
| Menu        | মেনু         |
| Order       | অর্ডার       |
| Waiter      | ওয়েটার      |
| Table       | টেবিল        |
| Bill        | বিল          |
| Tip         | বকশিশ        |
| Starter     | অ্যাপেটাইজার |
| Main course | মূল খাবার    |
| Dessert     | মিষ্টান্ন    |
| Drink       | পানীয়       |
| Reservation | বুকিং        |
| Hungry      | ক্ষুধার্ত    |
| Delicious   | সুস্বাদু     |
| Spicy       | ঝাল          |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Ordering Food

### 🍽️ Useful Sentences

* I’d like to see the menu, please.
* I’m ready to order.
* I’d like rice and chicken.
* Can I have a glass of water?
* Is this dish spicy?
* What do you recommend?
* I don’t eat beef.
* I’m vegetarian.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: During Eating

* This food is delicious.
* It tastes great.
* It’s very spicy.
* I like it.
* This is too salty.
* Can I get some water?

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: Asking for Bill

* Can I have the bill, please?
* Could you bring the bill?
* Is service included?
* Keep the change.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 5: Complaints

* My food is cold.
* This is not what I ordered.
* It’s too salty.
* Can you replace it, please?
* I’m not satisfied.

---

# 💬 80 Daily Speaking Sentences

## 🍽️ Restaurant Basics

1. I’m hungry.
2. Let’s go to a restaurant.
3. I want to eat something.
4. I like this place.
5. The menu looks good.
6. I’m ready to order.
7. What is popular here?
8. I’ll try this.
9. I’ll take the same.
10. That sounds good.

---

## 🍔 Ordering Food

11. I’d like rice and chicken.
12. I want a burger.
13. I want a pizza.
14. Can I get water?
15. Do you have vegetarian food?
16. Is this spicy?
17. I don’t like spicy food.
18. I’ll have this.
19. Anything special today?
20. That’s all.

---

## 🍽️ Dining

21. This is delicious.
22. It tastes great.
23. I love this food.
24. It’s too spicy.
25. It’s very tasty.
26. I like the flavor.
27. Can I get more rice?
28. This is enough.
29. I’m full.
30. I enjoyed the meal.

---

## 🧑‍🍳 Service

31. Waiter, please come here.
32. Excuse me.
33. Can you help me?
34. Please bring water.
35. Please hurry up.
36. Thank you.
37. Good service.
38. Everything is fine.
39. Please clean the table.
40. We are ready to leave.

---

## 💰 Payment

41. Can I have the bill?
42. Bring the bill, please.
43. Is tax included?
44. Here is the money.
45. Keep the change.
46. Can I pay by card?
47. I need a receipt.
48. Thank you for your service.
49. That’s all.
50. Have a nice day.

---

## 🍕 Extra Useful Sentences

51. I’m very hungry.
52. This restaurant is nice.
53. The food is fresh.
54. I want something light.
55. I don’t eat meat.
56. I’m allergic to peanuts.
57. This portion is big.
58. Can I share this?
59. I’ll come again.
60. I recommend this place.

---

## 🍔 More Daily Practice

61. I prefer chicken.
62. I like spicy food.
63. I don’t like oily food.
64. This is too hot.
65. The food is cold.
66. I need more sauce.
67. Please bring napkins.
68. The table is dirty.
69. Can we sit there?
70. I’m satisfied.

---

## 🍽️ Advanced Sentences

71. Could you recommend a dish?
72. What’s the special menu today?
73. I’d like something traditional.
74. This is not what I ordered.
75. Please replace it.
76. I think there is a mistake.
77. I’m not happy with this.
78. Can you fix it?
79. Thank you for your help.
80. We enjoyed everything.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Ordering Food

**Customer:** I’d like to see the menu, please.
**Waiter:** Here you are.
**Customer:** I’ll have rice and chicken.
**Waiter:** Anything to drink?
**Customer:** A glass of water, please.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Complaining

**Customer:** This food is cold.
**Waiter:** I’m sorry. I’ll replace it.
**Customer:** Thank you.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Restaurant Bill

**Customer:** Can I have the bill?
**Waiter:** Sure, here it is.
**Customer:** Keep the change.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Group Dining

**Friend:** What do you want to eat?
**You:** I want pizza.
**Friend:** Good choice!

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Recommendation

**Customer:** What do you recommend?
**Waiter:** Our special chicken curry.
**Customer:** I’ll try that.

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word       | Easy Pronunciation |
| ---------- | ------------------ |
| Restaurant | রেস-ট-রন্ট         |
| Menu       | মেন-ইউ             |
| Delicious  | ডি-লিশ-আস          |
| Beverage   | বেভ-রিজ            |
| Complaint  | কম-প্লেইন্ট        |
| Waiter     | ওয়েই-টার          |
| Receipt    | রি-সিট             |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips

❌ Give me food.
✅ I’d like to order food, please.

❌ Bill.
✅ Can I have the bill, please?

❌ Food bad.
✅ The food is not good.

---

# 🗣️ Speaking Challenge

নিচের বাক্যগুলো ৫ বার বলো:

1. I’d like to see the menu.
2. I’m ready to order.
3. This food is delicious.
4. Can I have the bill, please?
5. I’m not satisfied with this food.
6. What do you recommend?
7. I’ll take this.
8. Keep the change.
9. The food is too spicy.
10. Thank you for your service.

---

# 📝 Homework

## Part 1 – Writing (10–12 Sentences)

**"My Restaurant Experience"** লিখো:

* Where did you go?
* What did you eat?
* Did you like the food?
* Did you face any problem?

---

## Part 2 – Speaking

৩–৫ মিনিট রেস্টুরেন্টে খাবার অর্ডার করার মতো English practice করো।

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. “আমি মেনু দেখতে চাই”

A. I’d like to see the menu.
B. I see menu.
C. Show menu me.

---

### 2. “আমি অর্ডার দিতে প্রস্তুত”

A. I’m ready to order.
B. I order ready.
C. Ready I order.

---

### 3. “খাবার খুব সুস্বাদু”

A. The food is delicious.
B. Food good very.
C. Delicious food is.

---

### 4. “আমি বিল চাই”

A. Can I have the bill?
B. Give bill.
C. Bill me.

---

### 5. “আমি সন্তুষ্ট নই”

A. I’m not satisfied.
B. I not like food.
C. Not satisfied I am.

---

# 🌟 Daily Mission

আজ ১০ মিনিট practice করো:

### 🍽️ Restaurant Role-play

* I’d like to see the menu.
* I’ll order rice and chicken.
* Can I have the bill?

### 💬 Complaints Practice

* The food is cold.
* Please replace it.

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# ✅ Day 18: Travel Advanced English – Bus, Train, Flight & Direction Mastery

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🚗 Travel & Transport English উন্নত করা
* 🚌 Bus / Train / Flight Full Conversation
* 🗺️ Advanced Direction English
* 💬 80+ Daily Speaking Sentences
* 🎭 Real-life Travel Dialogues
* 🔊 Pronunciation Tips
* 📝 Homework
* ✅ Quiz

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Travel Vocabulary (Advanced)

| English        | বাংলা          |
| -------------- | -------------- |
| Departure      | প্রস্থান       |
| Arrival        | আগমন           |
| Platform       | প্ল্যাটফর্ম    |
| Terminal       | টার্মিনাল      |
| Boarding       | উঠা (যানবাহনে) |
| Delay          | বিলম্ব         |
| Cancelled      | বাতিল          |
| Ticket counter | টিকিট কাউন্টার |
| Route          | রুট            |
| Fare           | ভাড়া          |
| Transit        | যাত্রাপথ       |
| Stopover       | বিরতি স্টেশন   |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Bus Conversation

### 🚌 Buying Ticket

* I need a ticket to Dhaka.
* What time does the bus leave?
* Which platform is it?
* Is this seat available?
* How much is the fare?

---

### 🚌 On the Bus

* Does this bus go to Dhaka?
* Please stop here.
* How many stops are left?
* Is this seat taken?
* I want to get off here.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Train Conversation

* Which platform does the train leave from?
* What time is the train?
* Is this seat reserved?
* Where is the ticket counter?
* The train is delayed.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: Flight / Airport English

* I have a flight to Dubai.
* Where is the check-in counter?
* My flight is delayed.
* Where is Gate 12?
* I need boarding pass.
* Can I have a window seat?

---

# 🎯 Lesson 5: Asking Direction (Advanced)

* Could you please show me the way?
* How far is it from here?
* Is it within walking distance?
* Take the second left.
* Go straight for 500 meters.
* It’s opposite the bank.
* It’s next to the hospital.

---

# 💬 80 Daily Speaking Sentences

## 🚗 Travel Basics

1. I’m going to Dhaka.
2. I need a bus ticket.
3. What time does it leave?
4. Which platform is it?
5. I’m traveling today.
6. The journey is long.
7. I like traveling.
8. I’m going by train.
9. I’m going by bus.
10. I’m going by flight.

---

## 🚌 Bus

11. Where is the bus stop?
12. Is this seat free?
13. I want to get off here.
14. Please stop the bus.
15. The bus is late.
16. I missed the bus.
17. How much is the fare?
18. I need a ticket.
19. The bus is crowded.
20. Please wait.

---

## 🚆 Train

21. Where is the platform?
22. The train is delayed.
23. I have a ticket.
24. Is this seat reserved?
25. The train is coming.
26. The train is full.
27. I like train journeys.
28. It’s very fast.
29. I will get off here.
30. The station is big.

---

## ✈️ Flight

31. I have a flight.
32. My flight is at 10 a.m.
33. I need boarding pass.
34. Where is check-in?
35. My flight is delayed.
36. I’m waiting at the gate.
37. I have luggage.
38. I need help.
39. The flight is on time.
40. Please hurry.

---

## 🗺️ Direction

41. Go straight.
42. Turn left.
43. Turn right.
44. It’s nearby.
45. It’s far away.
46. It’s opposite the bank.
47. It’s next to the shop.
48. Take the second right.
49. Follow this road.
50. I need help.

---

## 💬 Extra Daily Sentences

51. I’m lost.
52. Can you help me?
53. Show me the way.
54. I don’t know this place.
55. How far is it?
56. I’m new here.
57. Please guide me.
58. I will walk.
59. I will take a taxi.
60. I need directions.

---

## 🧠 Advanced Travel English

61. The journey was smooth.
62. The bus was delayed.
63. The train is on time.
64. I missed my stop.
65. I reached safely.
66. I enjoyed the trip.
67. The road is busy.
68. The traffic is heavy.
69. I need a map.
70. I am traveling alone.

---

## 💡 More Useful Sentences

71. Please drop me here.
72. I’m in a hurry.
73. I’m waiting for bus.
74. I’ll arrive soon.
75. The station is crowded.
76. I lost my ticket.
77. I need information.
78. Thank you for your help.
79. Have a safe journey.
80. See you soon.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Bus Station

**A:** I need a ticket to Dhaka.
**B:** It’s 500 taka.
**A:** What time does it leave?
**B:** At 8 a.m.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Train Station

**A:** Which platform?
**B:** Platform 3.
**A:** Thank you.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Asking Direction

**A:** Excuse me, where is the hospital?
**B:** Go straight and turn left.
**A:** Thank you.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Flight

**A:** I have a flight to Dubai.
**B:** Show your passport, please.
**A:** Here it is.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Lost Situation

**A:** I’m lost. Can you help me?
**B:** Yes, where do you want to go?
**A:** To the bus station.

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word      | Easy Pronunciation |
| --------- | ------------------ |
| Departure | ডি-পার-চার         |
| Arrival   | অ্যা-রাই-ভাল       |
| Platform  | প্ল্যাট-ফর্ম       |
| Boarding  | বোর্ড-ইং           |
| Ticket    | টি-কেট             |
| Journey   | জার-নি             |
| Direction | ডাই-রেক-শন         |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips

❌ Where bus?
✅ Where is the bus stop?

❌ I go Dhaka.
✅ I am going to Dhaka.

❌ Show way.
✅ Could you please show me the way?

---

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. “আমি ঢাকায় যাচ্ছি”

A. I am going to Dhaka.
B. I go Dhaka.
C. I going Dhaka.

---

### 2. “বাস কখন ছাড়ে?”

A. What time does the bus leave?
B. When bus go?
C. Bus time?

---

### 3. “আমি হারিয়ে গেছি”

A. I’m lost.
B. I lost me.
C. Lost I am.

---

### 4. “প্ল্যাটফর্ম কোথায়?”

A. Where is the platform?
B. Platform where?
C. Where platform?

---

### 5. “সোজা যান এবং বামে ঘুরুন”

A. Go straight and turn left.
B. Straight go left turn.
C. Go left straight.

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# ✅ Day 19: Daily Conversation Mastery – Speak English Fluently (Real-Life Practice)

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 💬 Real-life Daily Conversation practice
* 🧠 English Thinking Technique
* 🔥 Fluency Building Method
* 🎭 Mixed Situation Speaking
* 🗣️ Natural Speaking Patterns
* 📝 Homework
* ✅ Speaking Test

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Think in English (Very Important 🔥)

আজ থেকে এই habit শুরু করো:

❌ আগে Bangla চিন্তা → তারপর English ❌
✅ সরাসরি English চিন্তা করো ✅

### Example:

❌ আমি বাজারে যাব
➡️ I will go to the market

❌ আমি এখন ব্যস্ত
➡️ I am busy now

❌ আমি খেতে চাই
➡️ I want to eat

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Daily Conversation Patterns

### 🟢 Greeting

* Hi! How are you?
* I’m fine, thank you.
* What about you?

---

### 🟢 Small Talk

* What are you doing now?
* I’m studying.
* I’m working.
* I’m relaxing.

---

### 🟢 Asking Questions

* Where are you going?
* What are you doing?
* Why are you late?
* How was your day?

---

### 🟢 Answers

* I’m going home.
* I’m going to work.
* I was busy.
* It was good.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Real-Life Mixed Situations

## 🏠 At Home

* I’m tired.
* I want to sleep.
* Please turn off the light.

---

## 🛍️ Outside

* How much is this?
* I’ll take it.
* It’s too expensive.

---

## 🚌 Travel

* I need a ticket.
* Where is the bus stop?
* I’m going to Dhaka.

---

## 💼 Office / Study

* I’m working on a project.
* I have an exam tomorrow.
* I need more time.

---

# 💬 80 Daily Speaking Sentences (Fluency Pack)

## 🗣️ Basic Daily English

1. I am fine.
2. I am busy.
3. I am tired.
4. I am happy.
5. I am hungry.
6. I am ready.
7. I am late.
8. I am free now.
9. I am learning English.
10. I am improving.

---

## 💬 Questions

11. What are you doing?
12. Where are you going?

14. Why are you sad?
15. When will you come?

17. What is this?
18. Are you ready?
19. Do you understand?
20. Can you help me?

## 🔄 Mixed Situations

66. I’m cooking food.
67. I’m cleaning my room.
68. I’m reading a book.
69. I’m playing a game.

## 💡 Natural Speaking

72. No problem.
73. Let’s go.
74. Come with me.
75. Be careful.
76. Take care.
77. See you later.
78. Have a nice day.
79. Good luck.
80. Stay safe.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 1 – Daily Conversation

**A:** Hi! How are you?
**B:** I’m fine. What about you?
**A:** I’m good too.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 2 – Mixed Life Situation

**A:** Where are you going?
**B:** I’m going to the market.
**A:** What will you buy?
**B:** I will buy food.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 3 – Study Life

**A:** Are you ready for the exam?
**B:** Not fully, I’m still studying.
**A:** Good luck!

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 4 – Help Situation

**A:** Can you help me?
**B:** Yes, sure.
**A:** Thank you so much.

---

# 🎭 Dialogue 5 – Casual Talk

**A:** What are you doing now?
**B:** I’m just relaxing.
**A:** Nice!

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word     | Easy Pronunciation |
| -------- | ------------------ |
| Busy     | বিজি               |
| Tired    | টাইয়ার্ড          |
| Ready    | রেডি               |
| Help     | হেল্প              |
| Learn    | লার্ন              |
| Improve  | ইমপ্রুভ            |
| Practice | প্র্যাকটিস         |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips (Fluency Secret 🔥)

👉 এক বাক্য বারবার practice করো
👉 English subtitles দিয়ে video দেখো
👉 প্রতিদিন 10–15 মিনিট English এ কথা বলো নিজের সাথে

---

# ✅ Mini Quiz

### 1. “আমি ব্যস্ত আছি”

A. I am busy.
B. I busy am.
C. Busy I am.

---

### 2. “আমি ইংরেজি শিখছি”

A. I am learning English.
B. I learn English.
C. English I learning.

---

### 3. “তুমি কি আমাকে সাহায্য করতে পারবে?”

A. Can you help me?
B. Help you me?
C. You help can me?

---

### 4. “চলো যাই”

A. Let’s go.
B. Go let’s.
C. Go we.

---

### 5. “আমি প্রস্তুত”

A. I am ready.
B. Ready I am.
C. I ready am.

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 🔥 Day 20: Fluency Boost Master Practice – Speak Without Thinking (Advanced Drill)

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🔥 English fluency বাড়ানো
* 🎤 Shadow Speaking Technique শেখা
* 🧠 Thinking in English আরও fast করা
* 🎭 Real conversation simulation
* ⚡ Speed speaking practice
* 📝 Speaking test (self-evaluation)

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Shadow Speaking Technique (Very Important 🔥)

👉 আমি বলব → তুমি সাথে সাথে repeat করবে

### Practice Set 1

* I am learning English.
* I am trying to speak fluently.
* I can do it.
* I will improve every day.

👉 লক্ষ্য: এক সেকেন্ডও pause না করা

---

### Practice Set 2

* What are you doing?
* I am studying.
* I am working hard.
* I am improving my English.

---

### Practice Set 3

* I need help.
* Please speak slowly.
* I don’t understand.
* Can you repeat that?

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Speed Speaking Drill ⚡

👉 দ্রুত বলার চেষ্টা করো (thinking time কমাও)

* I am busy now.
* I will call you later.
* I am going to the market.
* I am coming home.
* I am ready to go.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: English Thinking Expansion 🧠

আজ থেকে “Bangla translate” বন্ধ ❌

### Practice:

❌ আমি এখন খাচ্ছি
✅ I am eating now

❌ আমি ঘুমাতে চাই
✅ I want to sleep

❌ আমি ক্লাসে যাচ্ছি
✅ I am going to class

---

* I am busy.

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 🧠 Day 21: Grammar in Speaking – Tense in Real Life (Natural English)

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 💬 80+ Daily Speaking Sentences
* 🗣️ Fluency + Grammar together
* 📝 Homework
* ✅ Speaking Test

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Grammar in Speaking (Simple Rule)

👉 Grammar শেখার লক্ষ্য বই নয়
👉 লক্ষ্য = **Speaking fluency**

---

## 🟢 Present (Now)

👉 এখন যা হচ্ছে

* I am eating.
* I am studying.
* I go to school.
* I work every day.

---

## 🔵 Past (Before)

👉 যা আগে হয়েছে

* I ate rice.
* I went to school.
* I watched TV.
* I studied yesterday.

---

## 🔴 Future (Next)

👉 যা পরে হবে

* I will go to school.
* I will eat rice.
* I will call you.
* I will study tomorrow.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Real-Life Grammar Conversion

❌ ভুল → ✅ সঠিক

* I go yesterday ❌

* I went yesterday ✅

* I will went ❌

* I will go ✅

* I am go now ❌

* I am going now ✅

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Speaking Formula (Golden Rule 🔥)

👉 Use this formula:

### 🧠 Subject + Verb + Time

* I eat rice every day
* I ate rice yesterday
* I will eat rice tomorrow

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips (Very Important 🔥)

👉 Always think in sentence form
👉 Never translate word-by-word
👉 Practice 3 tenses daily
👉 Speak out loud (not silent reading)

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Speaking Test Rule (Important 🔥)

👉 আজ থেকে তুমি:

❌ Bangla translate করবে না
❌ Pause করে চিন্তা করবে না

✅ সরাসরি English এ বলবে

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Rapid Response Drill ⚡

👉 আমি প্রশ্ন দিচ্ছি → তুমি সাথে সাথে উত্তর দাও

* What are you doing? → I am studying.
* Where are you going? → I am going to market.
* Are you busy? → Yes, I am busy.
* Do you speak English? → Yes, I do.

---

* 💬 Fluency + Grammar mix practice
* 📝 Advanced homework challenge

-------
# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 🧠 Day 23: Sentence Building Master Class – Speak Complex English Naturally

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🧱 Sentence building skill উন্নত করা
* 🔥 Simple → Complex sentence বানানো
* 🎭 Real-life story speaking
* 🧠 Grammar + Fluency একসাথে ব্যবহার
* 💬 80+ advanced sentences
* 📝 Homework + speaking challenge

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Sentence Building Formula (Very Important 🔥)

👉 Basic structure:

### 🟢 Simple Sentence

* I go to school.

### 🔵 Add Time

* I go to school every day.

### 🔴 Add Reason / Detail

* I go to school every day because I want to learn.

### ⚡ Final Fluent Sentence

* I go to school every day because I want to improve my knowledge.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Expansion Technique 🧱

## Example 1

* I eat rice.
* I eat rice at night.
* I eat rice at night because I feel hungry.
* I eat rice at night because I feel very hungry after work.

---

## Example 2

* I study English.
* I study English every day.
* I study English every day to improve my fluency.
* I study English every day to improve my fluency and confidence.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Complex Sentence Patterns

### 🧠 Because (কারণ)

* I am happy because I passed the exam.

### 🧠 When (যখন)

* I was sleeping when he called me.

### 🧠 After (পরে)

* I went home after I finished my work.

### 🧠 Before (আগে)

* I wash my hands before I eat.

---

# 💬 80 Daily Sentence Building Pack

## 🟢 Basic Expansion

1. I go to school every day.
2. I go to school because I want to learn.
3. I go to school every day because I want a good future.
4. I am learning English.
5. I am learning English to improve my life.
6. I am learning English to get a good job.
7. I eat food.
8. I eat food when I am hungry.
9. I eat food when I come home.
10. I sleep at night.

---

## 🔵 Time-Based Sentences

11. I wake up early every day.
12. I wake up early to be productive.
13. I study at night.
14. I study at night because it is quiet.
15. I go out in the evening.
16. I go out when I feel bored.
17. I work in the morning.
18. I work in the morning to earn money.
19. I watch TV at night.
20. I watch TV after finishing my work.

---

## 🔴 Reason-Based Sentences

21. I am happy because I succeeded.
22. I am sad because I failed.
23. I am tired because I worked hard.
24. I am confident because I practice daily.
25. I am learning because I want success.
26. I am improving because I practice English.
27. I am busy because I have work.
28. I am free because today is holiday.
29. I am late because I missed the bus.
30. I am strong because I exercise.

---

## 🧠 Advanced Speaking

31. I am learning English every day to improve my communication skill.
32. I study hard because I want a better future.
33. I wake up early because I want to use my time well.
34. I go to market when I need something.
35. I call my friend when I feel lonely.
36. I read books because I want knowledge.
37. I work hard to achieve my goals.
38. I practice speaking English to become fluent.
39. I watch English videos to improve listening.
40. I try again when I fail.

---

## 🎭 Real-Life Sentences

41. I went to market after I finished my study.
42. I will go out when the rain stops.
43. I was sleeping when the phone rang.
44. I studied hard before the exam.
45. I will call you when I reach home.
46. I eat breakfast before going to school.
47. I feel happy when I speak English.
48. I learn faster when I practice daily.
49. I become confident when I speak English.
50. I improve when I make mistakes.

---

## 💬 Fluency Sentences

51. I am trying my best to improve my English speaking skill.
52. I am focused on becoming fluent in English.
53. I am practicing daily to build confidence.
54. I am learning step by step to master English.
55. I speak slowly so that I can be correct.
56. I repeat sentences to remember better.
57. I think in English to become fluent.
58. I avoid translation to speak faster.
59. I speak every day to improve.
60. I challenge myself to speak without fear.

---

## 🌟 Natural Daily English

61. Let’s go when you are ready.
62. I will wait until you come.
63. I stay home when I am tired.
64. I help my friend when he needs me.
65. I study after I finish dinner.
66. I relax when I finish work.
67. I smile when I am happy.
68. I stop when I am tired.
69. I continue when I feel strong.
70. I succeed when I never give up.

---

## 🚀 Master Level Sentences

71. I am improving my English speaking skill every day because I want to become fluent and confident.
72. I study English regularly so that I can communicate with anyone easily.
73. I practice speaking because I want to remove my hesitation.
74. I challenge myself every day to speak without thinking in Bangla.
75. I believe I can achieve fluency if I continue practicing daily.
76. I make mistakes but I learn from them.
77. I speak even if I am not perfect.
78. I don’t stop learning because success needs time.
79. I focus on progress, not perfection.
80. I am becoming better every single day.

---

# 🎭 Story Practice (Very Important 🎯)

👉 বলো নিজের সম্পর্কে:

* I wake up early in the morning.
* I go to study or work.
* I practice English every day.
* I make mistakes but I learn from them.
* I want to improve my life through English.

| Word     | Pronunciation |
| -------- | ------------- |
| Because  | বিকজ          |
| When     | হোয়েন        |
| After    | আফটার         |
| Before   | বিফোর         |
| Improve  | ইমপ্রুভ       |
| Practice | প্র্যাকটিস    |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips 🔥

👉 Simple → Complex বানাও
👉 এক বাক্য ৫ বার বলো
👉 “because / when / after” বেশি ব্যবহার করো
👉 English thinking চালু রাখো

---

4. I feel happy when I speak English.
5. I will succeed if I never give up.
6. I am improving every day.
7. I practice speaking daily.
8. I think in English now.
9. I can speak better than before.
10. I am becoming fluent.

-----------
# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 💬 Day 24: Daily Conversation Fluency Master – Real Talk Practice (Advanced Speaking)

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 💬 Real-life natural conversation fluency
* 🎭 Role-play situations (home, market, travel, friends)
* ⚡ Fast response English practice
* 🧠 Thinking in English stronger করা
* 🗣️ Natural speaking flow
* 📝 Homework + speaking test

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Real Conversation Formula 🔥

👉 Natural speaking pattern:

### 🧠 Short + Natural + Fast

❌ Long thinking
❌ Translation

✅ Direct response in English

---

## Example:

**Q:** What are you doing?
**A:** I’m studying.

**Q:** Where are you going?
**A:** I’m going to market.

**Q:** Are you busy?
**A:** Yes, a little.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Daily Real-Life Conversation Pack

## 🏠 Home Conversation

* I’m tired.
* I want to sleep.
* Please help me.
* I’ll do it later.
* I’m coming.

---

## 🛍️ Market Conversation

* How much is this?
* It’s too expensive.
* Give me discount.
* I’ll take it.
* Anything cheaper?

---

## 🚌 Travel Conversation

* I need a ticket.
* Where is the bus stop?
* I’m going to Dhaka.
* Please stop here.
* Is this seat free?

---

## 💬 Friend Conversation

* How are you?
* I’m fine.
* What are you doing?
* Nothing special.
* Let’s go out.

---

# 💬 80 Daily Fluency Sentences

5. I am happy.
6. I am sad.
7. I am ready.
8. I am late.
9. I am early.
10. I am okay.

## ⚡ Fast Responses

11. What are you doing? → I’m working.
12. Where are you going? → Home.
13. Are you busy? → Yes.
14. Are you free? → Yes.
15. Do you understand? → Yes.
16. Can you help me? → Yes.
17. Do you speak English? → Yes.
18. Are you ready? → Yes.
19. What is this? → I don’t know.
20. Where are you? → At home.

---

# 🎭 Role-play Practice

## 🏠 Home

**A:** Are you busy?
**B:** Yes, I am working.

---

## 🛍️ Market

**A:** How much is this?
**B:** 500 taka.
**A:** Too expensive.

---

## 🚌 Travel

**A:** Where are you going?
**B:** I’m going to Dhaka.

---

## 💬 Friends

**A:** What are you doing?
**B:** I’m relaxing.

---

## 🧠 Help Situation

**A:** Can you help me?
**B:** Yes, sure.

| ------- | ------------- |
| Busy    | বিজি          |
| Ready   | রেডি          |
| Try     | ট্রাই         |
| Speak   | স্পিক         |
| Learn   | লার্ন         |
| Improve | ইমপ্রুভ       |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips 🔥

👉 Short sentence = better fluency
👉 No translation in mind
👉 Daily repetition is key
👉 Speak out loud (not silent)

---

10. See you.

----------
# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 📖 Day 25: Storytelling Master Class – Speak English Like a Story (Fluency + Confidence)

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 📖 English storytelling শেখা
* 🎭 Past events naturally বলা
* 🔥 Fluency + grammar একসাথে ব্যবহার
* 🧠 Sentence flow তৈরি করা
* 💬 80+ storytelling sentences
* 📝 Homework + speaking test

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Storytelling Formula (Very Important 🔥)

👉 Story structure:

### 🟢 1. Start (Introduction)

* One day…
* Yesterday…
* Last week…

### 🔵 2. Event (What happened)

* I went to…
* I saw…
* I met…

### 🔴 3. Problem

* Suddenly…
* But…
* Unfortunately…

### 🟢 4. Ending

* Finally…
* In the end…
* I was happy…

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Simple Story Example

👉 My Day Story

* Yesterday I went to market.
* I bought some food.
* Suddenly it started raining.
* I got wet.
* Finally I came home and took rest.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Advanced Story Example 🔥

* Last week I went to Dhaka.
* I traveled by bus.
* Suddenly the bus broke down.
* We waited for 1 hour.
* Finally another bus came and we reached safely.
* I was tired but happy.

---

# 💬 80 Storytelling Sentences

## 🟢 Beginning Stories

1. One day I went out.
2. Yesterday I visited my friend.
3. Last week I traveled to Dhaka.
4. In the morning I woke up early.
5. At night I studied English.
6. Suddenly something happened.
7. It was a normal day.
8. I was very excited.
9. I had a strange experience.
10. I will never forget that day.

---

## 🔵 Actions in Story

11. I went to market.
12. I met my friend.
13. I saw a stranger.
14. I bought some food.
15. I traveled by bus.
16. I walked on the road.
17. I called my friend.
18. I waited for the bus.
19. I entered the shop.
20. I talked to the shopkeeper.

---

## 🔴 Problems in Story

21. Suddenly it started raining.
22. The bus was late.
23. I lost my wallet.
24. The road was blocked.
25. I felt sick.
26. I was confused.
27. The phone was dead.
28. I missed the bus.
29. I got lost.
30. I had no money.

---

## 🟢 Solutions / Ending

31. Finally I reached home.
32. In the end everything was fine.
33. I found my wallet.
34. I got help from a stranger.
35. The problem was solved.
36. I was safe.
37. I felt happy.
38. I learned a lesson.
39. I came back home.
40. Everything ended well.

---

## 🧠 Fluency Story Sentences

41. I had an interesting experience.
42. It was a memorable day.
43. I will never forget it.
44. It changed my thinking.
45. I learned something new.
46. I was very surprised.
47. I felt nervous.
48. I stayed calm.
49. I handled the situation.
50. I became confident.

---

## 🎭 Real-Life Story Flow

51. I woke up early.
52. I got ready.
53. I went outside.
54. I met my friend.
55. We went to market.
56. We bought food.
57. We talked a lot.
58. We had fun.
59. We came back home.
60. I rested.

---

## 🚀 Advanced Storytelling

61. I decided to go on a journey.
62. I prepared everything.
63. I started my trip.
64. I faced many challenges.
65. I stayed strong.
66. I did not give up.
67. I kept moving forward.
68. I solved problems one by one.
69. I reached my destination.
70. I felt proud.

---

## 🌟 Natural Story Endings

71. It was a great experience.
72. I enjoyed it a lot.
73. I learned a lesson from it.
74. I will remember it forever.
75. It was an amazing day.
76. I felt very happy.
77. I shared the story with my friend.
78. Everyone liked my story.
79. I smiled at the end.
80. Life goes on.

# 🎭 Full Story Practice

## 📖 My Market Story

* One day I went to market.
* I wanted to buy some food.
* I met my friend there.
* Suddenly it started raining.
* We took shelter in a shop.
* After some time the rain stopped.
* Finally I returned home safely.

---

# 🔊 Pronunciation Tips

| Word       | Pronunciation  |
| ---------- | -------------- |
| Suddenly   | সাডেনলি        |
| Finally    | ফাইনালি        |
| Experience | এক্সপিরিয়েন্স |
| Remember   | রিমেম্বার      |
| Journey    | জার্নি         |
| Problem    | প্রবলেম        |

---

# 💡 Speaking Tips 🔥

👉 Always use “One day / Yesterday / Suddenly / Finally”
👉 Speak like a movie story 🎬
👉 Don’t translate word by word
👉 Add emotions when speaking

---

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 🎤 Day 26: Job Interview English Mastery – Speak Confidently & Get Ready

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🎤 Job interview English শেখা
* 💼 Common interview questions + answers
* 🧠 Confidence building speaking practice
* 🔥 Self-introduction mastery
* 🎭 Mock interview practice
* 📝 Homework + speaking test

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Self Introduction (Most Important 🔥)

👉 Interview শুরু হয় self introduction দিয়ে

### 🟢 Simple Version

* My name is Md. Atiar Rahman.
* I am from Bangladesh.
* I am a student / fresher.
* I am learning English and programming.

---

### 🔥 Advanced Version

* My name is Md. Atiar Rahman.
* I am from Bangladesh.
* I am a passionate learner of English and technology.
* I am improving my skills in programming and communication.
* My goal is to build a successful career in IT.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Common Interview Questions 💼

## ❓ Tell me about yourself

👉 Answer:

* I am a hardworking and dedicated person.
* I am learning English and programming.
* I want to build my career in IT.

---

## ❓ What are your strengths?

👉 Answer:

* I am a quick learner.
* I am hardworking.
* I never give up easily.

---

## ❓ What are your weaknesses?

👉 Answer:

* I sometimes feel nervous, but I am improving.
* I am working on my communication skills.

---

## ❓ Why should we hire you?

👉 Answer:

* I am dedicated and honest.
* I am eager to learn.
* I will give my best effort.

---

## ❓ What is your goal?

👉 Answer:

* My goal is to become a skilled professional in IT.
* I want to build a successful career.

---

# 💬 Day 27: Advanced Conversation Mastery – Real-Life Problem Solving English

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Problem-Solving English Formula 🔥

👉 যখন সমস্যা হবে, এই structure ব্যবহার করো:

### 🧠 Step 1: Explain problem

* I have a problem.
* Something is wrong.

### 🧠 Step 2: Describe situation

* My phone is not working.
* The bus is late.

### 🧠 Step 3: Ask help

* Can you help me?
* What should I do?

### 🧠 Step 4: Solution

* Thank you for your help.
* Now it is fixed.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Real-Life Problem Situations 🎭

## 📱 Phone Problem

* My phone is not working.
* I can’t call anyone.
* Can you help me?

---

## 🚌 Travel Problem

* The bus is late.
* I missed my stop.
* What should I do?

---

## 💰 Money Problem

* I don’t have enough money.
* Can I get a discount?
* I need help.

---

## 🏠 Home Problem

* The light is not working.
* I need help to fix it.
* Please help me.

---

# 💬 80 Daily Problem-Solving Sentences

## 🟢 Basic Problems

1. I have a problem.
2. Something is wrong.

6. I am confused.
7. I am stuck.

## 🏠 Home Issue

**B:** I will fix it.

**A:** Can you help me?
**B:** Yes, sure.

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 🌟 Day 32: Native-Like Conversation Patterns – Speak Naturally & Smoothly

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🧠 Native-like sentence patterns শেখা
* 💬 Natural conversation flow তৈরি করা

* 🎭 Real-life dialogue mastery

* 🗣️ Fluent daily speaking upgrade

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Native Speaking Rule 🔥

👉 Native speakers কীভাবে কথা বলে:

❌ Very formal English
❌ Long sentences always

✅ Short + natural + flexible
✅ Everyday expressions
✅ Fast response

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Natural Conversation Patterns 🎭

## 🟢 Pattern 1: Short Answer + Expansion

**Q:** Are you busy?
**A:** Yes, a bit. I’m working.

**Q:** Where are you going?
**A:** Home. I need rest.

---

## 🟢 Pattern 2: Natural Agreement

* That’s true.
* I think so too.
* Exactly.
* I agree with you.

---

## 🟢 Pattern 3: Natural Thinking

* Let me think.
* I’m not sure yet.
* I guess so.
* Probably yes.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Real-Life Native Conversations 🎭

## 🏠 Home Talk

* I’ll rest for a while.

* I’ll take it.

---

## 🚌 Travel Talk

* I’m heading home.
* I’ll take the bus.
* It won’t take long.

---

## 💬 Friend Talk

* What’s up?
* Not much.
* Let’s hang out.

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Emotional Speaking Rule 🔥

👉 Native speakers শুধু শব্দ বলে না—emotion express করে

### ❌ Flat English

* I am sad.

### ✅ Emotional English

* I feel really sad today…

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Emotion Words Pack 🧠

## 😊 Happy

* I am so happy.
* I feel amazing.
* I’m really excited.

## 😢 Sad

* I feel really down.
* I’m a bit upset.
* I feel broken inside.

## 😡 Angry

* I’m really angry.
* I can’t believe this.
* This is so frustrating.

## 😍 Love / Care

* I really care about you.
* I miss you a lot.
* You mean a lot to me.

## 😰 Nervous

* I feel nervous.
* I’m a bit worried.
* My heart is beating fast.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Emotional Sentence Building 🎭

## 🟢 Simple

* I failed the exam.

## 🔵 Emotional

* I failed the exam… I feel really disappointed.

## 🔴 Advanced

* I worked so hard, but I failed the exam… I feel really broken, but I will try again.

---

* I feel stronger now.
* I express my emotions.
* I understand myself better.
* I am improving every day.

👉 Real feeling connect করো

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 🎤 Day 35: Persuasion & Debate Speaking – Speak Confidently & Convince Others

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🧠 Persuasion (convince) English শেখা
* 💬 Opinion + argument structure
* 🔥 Confidence speaking boost
* 🎭 Real-life discussion practice
* 🗣️ Fluent reasoning skill

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Debate Speaking Rule 🔥

👉 Debate মানে শুধু English বলা না—
👉 তোমার opinion strong করে বলা

### 🧠 Structure:

1. Opinion (মতামত)
2. Reason (কারণ)
3. Example (উদাহরণ)
4. Conclusion (শেষ কথা)

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Basic Debate Expressions 🎤

## 🟢 Agree (সম্মতি)

* I agree with you.
* That’s a good point.
* I think so too.

## 🔴 Disagree (অসম্মতি)

* I don’t think so.
* I disagree with you.
* I’m not sure about that.

## 🧠 Opinion

* I believe that…
* In my opinion…
* I think that…

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Persuasion English 🔥

👉 কাউকে convince করার ভাষা:

* You should try this.
* I strongly believe that…
* It is better to…
* Let me explain why…

---

# 💬 80 Debate & Opinion Sentences

## 🧠 Opinion Start

1. I think this is important.
2. I believe it is true.
3. In my opinion, this is good.
4. I feel this is right.
5. I strongly believe this.
6. I think we should try it.
7. I don’t agree with this.
8. I have a different opinion.
9. This is my point of view.
10. I see it differently.

---

## 🔥 Agree / Disagree

11. I agree with you.
12. That’s true.
13. Exactly.
14. I think so too.
15. I don’t think so.
16. I disagree.
17. I’m not sure.
18. That may be true.
19. I respect your opinion.
20. I see your point.

---

## 🧠 Reasoning

21. Because it is helpful.
22. Because it is useful.
23. Because it improves life.
24. Because it saves time.
25. Because it is better.
26. That’s why I think so.
27. This is the reason.
28. It makes sense.
29. It helps people.
30. It is important.

---

## 🎤 Persuasion Lines

31. You should try this.
32. Let me explain.
33. I suggest that you try it.
34. I recommend this.
35. It is better to do it.
36. You will benefit from it.
37. Trust me on this.
38. Think about it.
39. Give it a try.
40. You will see the result.

---

## 💬 Real Debate English

41. I think social media is helpful.
42. I believe education is important.
43. I don’t agree with this idea.
44. Technology is improving life.
45. Hard work leads to success.
46. Practice makes perfect.
47. English is very important.
48. Communication is the key.
49. Time management is important.
50. Learning never stops.

---

## 🚀 Advanced Opinion

51. I strongly believe in this idea.
52. This is the best solution.
53. I completely agree with it.
54. I partially agree.
55. I have strong reasons.
56. Let me clarify my point.
57. This is logical.
58. It is very effective.
59. I support this idea.
60. I stand by my opinion.

---

## 🌟 Fluent Debate Style

61. From my perspective, this is correct.
62. I see it as a better option.
63. I think we should consider it.
64. This is not the right approach.
65. I feel it can be improved.
66. There are better solutions.
67. We should think again.
68. This works well.
69. It might not be effective.
70. I believe in this approach.

---

## 🔥 Master Level Speaking

75. I defend my opinion.

78. I communicate effectively.

80. I am becoming a fluent speaker.

# 🎯 Lesson 1: IELTS Speaking Structure 🔥

👉 যেকোনো প্রশ্নে এই structure follow করো:

### 🧠 Answer Formula:

1. Direct Answer (Yes/No or main idea)
2. Explanation (Why)
3. Example (Real life)
4. Opinion (Your view)

---

# 🎤 Example Question

👉 Do you like learning English?

### 🟢 Answer:

* Yes, I do.
* Because it helps me communicate globally.
* I practice English every day with videos and speaking.
* I think it is very important for my future.

## 🌍 Topic 4: Technology

* Technology is very useful.
* It makes life easier.
* I use mobile and computer daily.
* I think it will improve more in future.

# 💬 80 IELTS Speaking Sentences

# 💡 Speaking Tips 🔥

👉 Structure follow করো (Answer + Reason + Example + Opinion)
👉 Always give example
👉 Don’t memorize, understand
👉 Speak slowly but clearly

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 🏆 Day 39: IELTS Part 2 + Advanced Discussion Mastery (Final Upgrade Level)

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🎤 IELTS Part 2 long speaking (2-minute answer)
* 🧠 Structured + logical speaking control
* 💬 Advanced discussion + storytelling mix
* 🔥 Confidence under pressure
* ⚡ Fluent continuous speech
* 🗣️ Native-like organized English

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: IELTS Part 2 FINAL STRUCTURE 🔥

👉 যেকোনো topic এ 2-minute answer এর formula:

### 🧠 PERFECT STRUCTURE:

1. Introduction (topic introduce)
2. Background (when/where)
3. Details (what happened)
4. Opinion (what you think)
5. Emotion (how you feel)
6. Conclusion (final thought)

---

# 🎤 Example (Very Important)

👉 Topic: A difficult situation in your life

* I would like to talk about a difficult situation in my life.
* It happened during my academic life.
* I was struggling with my studies.
* I think I didn’t manage my time well.
* I felt very stressed and disappointed.
* But I learned a lot from it and improved myself.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Advanced Discussion Upgrade 🎭

👉 Real speaking flow:

* I think this is very important.
* Because it helps people grow.
* For example, I practice English daily.
* That’s why my confidence is improving.
* I believe consistency is the key.

---

# 💬 80 IELTS + Advanced Speaking Sentences

## 🧠 Introduction Lines

1. I would like to talk about…
2. I want to describe…
3. Let me explain…
4. Today I will discuss…
5. I remember a situation…
6. This topic is about…
7. I have experience of…
8. I would like to share…
9. It was an important moment…
10. I will talk about it clearly…

---

## 🎭 Story Development

11. It happened some time ago.
12. I was in a difficult situation.
13. I didn’t know what to do.
14. I felt very confused.
15. I tried to stay calm.
16. I made a decision.
17. I took action quickly.
18. I kept trying again.
19. I didn’t give up.
20. I focused on solution.

---

## 💬 Detail Expansion

21. The situation was serious.
22. I had no clear idea.
23. I needed support.
24. I worked very hard.
25. I changed my plan.
26. I improved slowly.
27. I practiced regularly.
28. I stayed consistent.
29. I gained confidence.
30. I learned a lot.

---

## 🔥 Emotion + Opinion

31. I felt really nervous.
32. I was under pressure.
33. I felt disappointed.
34. I felt motivated again.
35. I felt proud later.
36. I think it was a good experience.
37. I realized my mistakes.
38. I became stronger.
39. I gained experience.
40. I improved myself.

---

## 🧠 Linking Words (Very Important)

41. Because of that…
42. As a result…
43. Therefore…
44. However…
45. In addition…
46. On the other hand…
47. That’s why…
48. For this reason…
49. Eventually…
50. At that moment…

---

## 🚀 Fluency Boost Sentences

51. I can speak more fluently now.
52. I organize my thoughts better.
53. I express ideas clearly.
54. I don’t hesitate anymore.
55. I think in English now.
56. I respond faster.
57. I feel confident speaking.
58. I improve every day.
59. I practice regularly.
60. I stay focused.

---

## 🌟 Master Level Speaking

61. I can handle complex topics.
62. I manage speaking pressure.
63. I stay calm while speaking.
64. I build structured answers.
65. I give clear explanations.
66. I support my ideas properly.
67. I use natural English.
68. I speak without fear.
69. I improve continuously.
70. I am becoming fluent.

---

## 🎯 IELTS Final Level Sentences

71. I can speak for two minutes easily.
72. I can describe any situation.
73. I can express my opinion clearly.
74. I can answer under pressure.
75. I can give real-life examples.
76. I can stay confident always.
77. I can organize my speech.

79. I am ready for real exams.
80. I am mastering English speaking.

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 🏆 Day 40: FULL IELTS MOCK TEST – Complete Speaking Exam Simulation

🎉 আজকের দিনটা খুব গুরুত্বপূর্ণ!
আজ তুমি real IELTS speaking exam এর মতো practice করবে।

---

# 🎯 আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🏆 Full IELTS Speaking Mock Test (Part 1 + 2 + 3)
* 🎤 Time-based speaking control
* 🧠 Pressure handling skill
* 💬 Natural + structured answers
* 🔥 Confidence building under exam condition
* 🗣️ Real interview-level English

---

# 🎯 RULES OF TODAY 🔥

❌ Pause করা যাবে না
❌ Bangla চিন্তা করা যাবে না
❌ Word-by-word translation বন্ধ

✅ Only English speaking
✅ Short + clear sentences
✅ Natural flow

---

# 🎤 PART 1: Introduction (Basic Questions)

👉 Answer quickly:

### 🧠 Questions:

* What is your name?
* Where are you from?
* Do you like learning English?
* What do you do?

### 💬 Sample Answers:

* My name is Atiar.
* I am from Bangladesh.
* Yes, I like learning English.
* I am a student / learner.

---

# 🎤 PART 2: Long Speaking (2 Minutes)

👉 Topic: Describe a difficult situation in your life

### 🧠 Structure:

1. Introduction
2. Situation
3. Problem
4. Action
5. Result
6. Learning

---

### 💬 Sample Answer:

* I would like to talk about a difficult situation in my life.
* It happened during my studies.
* I was struggling with my exams.
* I didn’t manage my time properly.
* I decided to work harder and improve.
* I practiced daily and stayed focused.
* Finally, I improved my results.
* I learned that discipline is very important.

---

# 🎤 PART 3: Discussion (Advanced Questions)

## 🧠 Q1: Why is English important?

* English is very important.
* Because it helps global communication.
* It improves career opportunities.
* I think it is necessary for success.

---

## 🧠 Q2: How can people improve speaking?

* People can improve by practice.
* They should speak daily.
* Watching English content helps a lot.
* Consistency is very important.

---

## 🧠 Q3: Do you think education is important?

* Yes, I do.
* Education builds our future.
* It gives knowledge and skills.
* I strongly believe it is essential.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Interview Answer Formula 🔥

👉 যেকোনো প্রশ্নে এই structure follow করো:

### 🧠 STRUCTURE:

1. Direct Answer (short)
2. Explanation (why)
3. Example (experience/skill)
4. Confidence closing line

---

# 🎤 Lesson 2: Self Introduction (VERY IMPORTANT)

👉 Example:

* My name is Atiar.
* I am a student and a learner of English and programming.
* I am improving my communication and technical skills.
* I am a quick learner and hardworking person.
* I want to build my career in IT.

* I always try to improve myself.

---

## 🧠 Q3: What are your weaknesses?

* I sometimes feel nervous.
* But I am working on improving it.
* I practice speaking daily.

---

## 🧠 Q4: Why should we hire you?

* I am a quick learner.
* I am motivated and hardworking.
* I am ready to learn new things.
* I will give my best effort.

---

## 🧠 Q5: What are your goals?

* My goal is to build a career in IT.
* I want to become a skilled developer.
* I am working hard every day.

# 🏢 Day 42: Corporate English Mastery – Office Communication & Professional Fluency

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Corporate English Style 🔥

👉 Office English সবসময়:

❌ Too casual English না
❌ Slang না

✅ Polite + clear + professional

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Office Communication Rules 🏢

### 🧠 Always use:

* Could you please…
* I would like to…
* Please let me know…
* I appreciate your help

---

# 💼 Lesson 3: Office Conversation Examples 🎤

## 👨‍💼 Asking for Work

* Could you please send me the file?
* I would like to complete this task.
* Please give me the details.

---

## 📧 Email Style English

* I hope you are doing well.
* I am writing to inform you…
* Please find the attached file.
* Looking forward to your response.

---

## 🤝 Team Communication

* Let’s work together on this.
* I agree with your idea.
* That’s a good suggestion.
* We should finish this on time.

---

## ⏰ Deadline / Work Pressure

* I will complete it by today.
* I need some more time.
* I am working on it.
* I will submit it soon.

---

# 💬 80 Corporate English Sentences

## 🏢 Office Basics

1. I am working on this task.
2. I will complete it soon.
3. Please check this.
4. I need your help.
5. I am available now.
6. I am busy with work.
7. I will update you.
8. Let’s discuss it.
9. I agree with you.
10. I understand the task.

---

## 📧 Email / Formal Style

11. I hope you are well.
12. I am writing to inform you.
13. Please find attached file.
14. Looking forward to your reply.
15. Thank you for your support.
16. Please let me know.
17. I would like to request.
18. Kindly check this.
19. I appreciate your help.
20. Best regards.

---

## 🤝 Teamwork Communication

21. Let’s work together.
22. We should complete this.
23. I agree with your idea.
24. That’s a great suggestion.
25. We can improve this.
26. Let’s discuss more.
27. I support your plan.
28. We are on the same page.
29. Good teamwork.
30. Let’s finalize it.

---

## ⏰ Work Management

31. I will finish it today.
32. I need more time.
33. I am almost done.
34. I will submit soon.
35. I am working on it.
36. I will update you soon.
37. Please wait a moment.
38. I will handle it.
39. I am prioritizing this.
40. It is in progress.

---

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 🎤 Day 43: Advanced Presentation + Public Speaking Mastery (Corporate Level Upgrade)

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Presentation Structure 🔥

👉 যেকোনো presentation এ এই structure follow করো:

### 🧠 5-Step Formula:

1. Introduction (Topic introduce)
2. Objective (Why you are speaking)
3. Main Points (Key ideas)
4. Explanation (Details)
5. Conclusion (Summary)

---

# 🎤 Example Presentation

👉 Topic: Importance of English

* Good morning everyone.
* Today I will talk about importance of English.
* English is very important for communication.
* It helps in education and career.
* So we should practice English daily.

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Public Speaking Rules 🎤

## 🧠 Speak Like a Leader:

* Speak slowly
* Use clear sentences
* Maintain eye contact (imaginary)
* Don’t rush
* Be confident

---

# 💼 Lesson 3: Meeting English 🎯

## 🧠 Useful Phrases:

* Let’s start the meeting.
* I would like to share my idea.
* I agree with this point.
* I have a suggestion.
* Let’s finalize this.

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Mixed Speaking Formula 🔥

👉 আজকে যেকোনো প্রশ্নে 3-in-1 style use করো:

### 🧠 STRUCTURE:

1. Opinion (What you think)
2. Reason (Why)
3. Example / Experience
4. Conclusion (Final statement)

---

# 🎤 Example (Very Important)

* I think English is very important.
* Because it helps global communication.
* For example, I use English in learning and practice.
* So I believe it is essential for success.

* So we should improve it daily.

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Advanced Emotional Story Formula 🔥

👉 আজ তুমি কথা বলবে এই structure এ:

### 🧠 6-Step Formula:

1. Situation (কি ঘটেছিল)
2. Problem (সমস্যা কী ছিল)
3. Feeling (তুমি কেমন অনুভব করেছিলে)
4. Action (তুমি কী করেছিলে)
5. Result (ফলাফল কী হলো)
6. Learning (কি শিখলে)

---

# 🎤 Example Story

* I improved my study habits.
* I learned that consistency is very important.

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Native Speaking Rule 🔥

👉 আজ থেকে তুমি:

❌ বাক্য আগে বানাবে না
❌ বাংলায় চিন্তা করবে না

✅ শুধু English “idea” চিন্তা করবে
✅ তারপর সরাসরি বলবে
✅ Simple + natural sentence ব্যবহার করবে

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Instant Response Formula ⚡

👉 যেকোনো প্রশ্নে:

### 🧠 3-Step Method:

1. Direct Answer
2. Short Reason
3. Simple Example

---

# 🎤 Example

👉 Do you like English?

* Yes, I do.
* Because it helps my future.
* I practice it every day.

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Real Spontaneous Questions 🎤

* Do you like studying?
* What is your goal?
* How do you feel today?
* What is your dream job?

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Real-World Speaking Rule 🔥

👉 আজকের নিয়ম:

❌ না থেমে চিন্তা করা
❌ লম্বা sentence বানানো

✅ ছোট sentence
✅ দ্রুত উত্তর
✅ natural flow

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: 3-Second Response Formula ⚡

👉 যেকোনো situation:

### 🧠 STRUCTURE:

1. Direct Answer
2. Short Detail
3. Optional Example

---

# 🎤 Example

👉 Where are you going?

* I am going home.
* I am a bit tired.
* I will rest there.

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Ultimate Mixed Speaking Formula 🔥

👉 আজ তুমি যেকোনো প্রশ্নে এই structure use করবে:

### 🧠 4-Step Formula:

1. Opinion (What you think)
2. Reason (Why)
3. Example (Real life / imagination)
4. Final conclusion

---

# 🎤 Example (Very Important)

👉 Is failure good for success?

* I think failure is important for success.
* Because it helps us learn from mistakes.
* For example, I failed once in studies but improved later.
* So I believe failure is part of success.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Interview + Debate + Story Mix 🎤

## 💼 Interview Question

👉 Why do you want this job?

* I want this job because I want to build my career.
* I am a quick learner and hardworking person.
* For example, I improve my skills daily.
* So I believe I can contribute well.

---

## 🎤 Debate Question

👉 Internet is good or bad?

* I think internet is very useful.
* Because it helps in education and communication.
* For example, I learn English from online resources.
* But we should use it in a balanced way.

---

## 🎭 Story Question

👉 Describe a challenge you faced

* I faced a big challenge in my studies.
* I felt stressed and confused.
* I decided to work harder and improve.
* I practiced daily and stayed consistent.
* Finally, I succeeded and learned a lot.

---

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 🏆 Day 49: Final Speaking Test Simulation (IELTS + Interview + Corporate)

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🎤 Real exam-style speaking test
* 💼 Job interview practice

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Universal Speaking Formula

যেকোনো প্রশ্নের উত্তর এই 5-step structure-এ দাও:

1. **Direct Answer**
2. **Reason**
3. **Example**
4. **Personal Experience**
5. **Conclusion**

### Example

**Question:** Why are you learning English?

**Answer:**

> I am learning English because it is an international language. It helps me communicate with people from different countries. For example, I use English while studying programming and watching online tutorials. It also increases my confidence. That's why I practice English every day.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: IELTS Speaking Simulation

## Part 1 (Short Answers)

Answer these questions naturally.

### Questions

1. What do you do?
2. Why are you learning English?
3. How often do you practice speaking?
4. What do you usually do in your free time?
5. Do you enjoy reading books?

### Sample Answer

> I am a student and I am learning programming. I practice English every day because I want to become fluent. In my free time, I watch educational videos and build programming projects.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: IELTS Part 2

## Topic

**Describe a skill you want to improve.**

### Sample Answer

> I would like to improve my English speaking skill. I started learning English because I want to communicate confidently and work in the IT industry. At first, speaking was difficult for me because I translated everything from Bangla. Later, I started practicing every day. Now I feel much more confident, but I still want to become fluent.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: IELTS Part 3 (Discussion)

### Question

Is learning English important nowadays?

### Sample Answer

> Yes, I think English is very important because it is used all over the world. It helps people communicate, study abroad, and get better job opportunities. I believe English opens many doors for personal and professional growth.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 5: Job Interview Simulation

## Question 1

Tell me about yourself.

### Sample Answer

> My name is Atiar Rahman. I am passionate about programming and continuous learning. Currently, I am improving my English communication skills alongside learning Python, Django, and machine learning. I enjoy solving problems and building practical projects.

---

## Question 2

Why should we hire you?

### Sample Answer

> I am hardworking, responsible, and always willing to learn. I adapt quickly to new technologies and enjoy working in a team. I believe I can contribute positively to the company while continuing to improve my skills.

---

## Question 3

Where do you see yourself in five years?

### Sample Answer

> In five years, I see myself as an experienced software engineer working on challenging projects. I also want to continue learning new technologies and contribute to meaningful products.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 6: Corporate Meeting Practice

### Situation

Your manager asks for a project update.

### Example Conversation

**Manager:** Can you give me an update on the project?

**You:** Certainly. I have completed the backend API, and I am currently working on authentication. I expect to finish this phase by Friday. If everything goes as planned, we can begin testing next week.

---

# 💬 50 High-Level Speaking Sentences

### Giving Opinions

1. I completely agree.
2. I partially agree.
3. In my opinion...
4. From my perspective...
5. I strongly believe...
6. I don't think that's true.
7. It depends on the situation.
8. There are several reasons.
9. I would say that...
10. Personally...

### Explaining Ideas

12. One important factor is...
13. Another point is...
14. For example...
15. For instance...
16. This helps because...
17. As a result...
18. Therefore...
19. Consequently...
20. Overall...

### Professional English

### Fluency Boost

32. That's a good question.
33. Let me think for a moment.
34. From my experience...
35. I have noticed that...
36. I have learned that...
37. I believe practice is the key.
38. I continue improving every day.
39. I enjoy speaking English.
40. I feel more confident now.

44. Furthermore...
45. In addition...

# 💡 Today's Speaking Tips

✅ Speak slowly and clearly.

✅ Don't memorize answers word for word.

✅ If you forget a word, explain it using easier English.

✅ Use linking words:

* First
* Then
* After that
* Finally
* Therefore
* However
* In addition

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 🚀 Day 50: Native English Conversation – Idioms, Phrasal Verbs & Natural Expressions

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🗣️ Native-এর মতো natural English বলা
* 🔥 Common idioms শেখা
* ⚡ Daily phrasal verbs ব্যবহার করা
* 💬 Natural conversation expressions
* 🎤 Sound more fluent and confident
* 🧠 Think and respond like an advanced English speaker

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Sound Natural in English

Native speakers সবসময় textbook English ব্যবহার করে না।

❌ I am very tired.

✅ I'm exhausted.

---

❌ I understand.

✅ I got it.

---

❌ That's very easy.

✅ It's a piece of cake.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: 20 Common Idioms

| Idiom                         | Meaning           | Example                                          |
| ----------------------------- | ----------------- | ------------------------------------------------ |
| Break the ice                 | কথা শুরু করা      | Let's play a game to break the ice.              |
| Piece of cake                 | খুব সহজ           | The exam was a piece of cake.                    |
| Hit the books                 | মনোযোগ দিয়ে পড়া | I need to hit the books tonight.                 |
| Once in a blue moon           | খুব কম            | I eat fast food once in a blue moon.             |
| Better late than never        | দেরি হলেও ভালো    | Better late than never.                          |
| Under the weather             | অসুস্থ লাগা       | I feel under the weather today.                  |
| Costs an arm and a leg        | খুব দামি          | That phone costs an arm and a leg.               |
| Miss the boat                 | সুযোগ হারানো      | Don't miss the boat.                             |
| Call it a day                 | আজকের কাজ শেষ     | Let's call it a day.                             |
| Kill two birds with one stone | একসাথে দুই কাজ    | I walk to work to kill two birds with one stone. |
| On the same page              | একই মত            | We are on the same page.                         |
| Burn the midnight oil         | রাত জেগে কাজ করা  | I burned the midnight oil yesterday.             |
| Hit the nail on the head      | ঠিক কথা বলা       | You hit the nail on the head.                    |
| Keep an eye on                | নজর রাখা          | Please keep an eye on my bag.                    |
| Pull someone's leg            | মজা করা           | I'm just pulling your leg.                       |
| Bite the bullet               | কঠিন কাজ শুরু করা | I decided to bite the bullet.                    |
| Cut corners                   | শর্টকাট নেওয়া    | Don't cut corners.                               |
| Get over it                   | ভুলে যাও          | You'll get over it.                              |
| Hang in there                 | ধৈর্য ধরো         | Hang in there.                                   |
| Take it easy                  | আরাম করো          | Take it easy today.                              |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: 20 Daily Phrasal Verbs

| Phrasal Verb | Meaning             | Example                      |
| ------------ | ------------------- | ---------------------------- |
| Wake up      | ঘুম থেকে ওঠা        | I wake up at 6.              |
| Get up       | বিছানা ছাড়া        | I get up quickly.            |
| Turn on      | চালু করা            | Turn on the light.           |
| Turn off     | বন্ধ করা            | Turn off the fan.            |
| Pick up      | তুলে নেওয়া         | Pick up your phone.          |
| Put down     | রেখে দেওয়া         | Put down the book.           |
| Look for     | খোঁজা               | I'm looking for my keys.     |
| Find out     | জানতে পারা          | I found out the answer.      |
| Go on        | চালিয়ে যাওয়া      | Please go on.                |
| Give up      | ছেড়ে দেওয়া        | Never give up.               |
| Carry on     | চালিয়ে যাওয়া      | Carry on your work.          |
| Come back    | ফিরে আসা            | Come back soon.              |
| Sit down     | বসা                 | Please sit down.             |
| Stand up     | দাঁড়ানো            | Stand up, please.            |
| Take off     | খুলে ফেলা / উড্ডয়ন | The plane took off.          |
| Put on       | পরা                 | Put on your shoes.           |
| Work out     | অনুশীলন করা         | I work out every morning.    |
| Run into     | হঠাৎ দেখা হওয়া     | I ran into my teacher.       |
| Look after   | যত্ন নেওয়া         | She looks after her parents. |
| Check out    | দেখে নেওয়া         | Check out this website.      |

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: Natural Conversation Expressions

### Greeting

* How's it going?
* What's up?
* Nice to see you.
* Long time no see.
* Good to see you again.

---

### Agreeing

* Absolutely.
* Exactly.
* You're right.
* I couldn't agree more.
* That's true.

---

### Disagreeing Politely

* I don't think so.
* I'm not sure about that.
* I see your point, but...
* That's one way to look at it.
* I have a different opinion.

---

### Thinking Time

Instead of saying "Ummm..."

Say:

* Let me think.
* That's a good question.
* Give me a second.
* Let me see.
* Well...

---

# 🎯 Lesson 5: Real Conversation

## Friend Conversation

**A:** Hey! How's it going?

**B:** Pretty good. What about you?

**A:** I'm doing well.

**B:** What have you been up to?

**A:** I've been learning English and programming.

**B:** That's awesome!

**A:** Thanks! I'm trying my best.

---

# 💬 50 Natural English Sentences

### Daily English

1. I'm doing great.
2. I'm a bit busy.
3. No worries.
4. Sounds good.
5. That's awesome.
6. I totally agree.
7. Not a problem.
8. Let's do it.
9. That's interesting.
10. I'm excited.

### Conversation

11. What do you think?
12. How was your day?
13. Tell me more.
14. Really?
15. Seriously?
16. That's amazing.
17. I didn't know that.
18. Good idea.
19. That's perfect.
20. Exactly.

### Workplace

21. I'll take care of it.
22. I'll get back to you.
23. Let's discuss this.
24. I'm working on it.
25. Thank you for your feedback.
26. I appreciate your help.
27. I'll update you soon.
28. I'll finish it today.
29. Let's move forward.
30. Good teamwork.

### Fluency

31. Let me explain.
32. In my opinion...
33. For example...
34. I believe...
35. However...
36. Therefore...
37. In addition...
38. Overall...
39. That's why...
40. Finally...

### Confidence

41. I can do it.
42. I believe in myself.
43. Every day is a new opportunity.
44. Practice makes progress.
45. I never stop learning.
46. Mistakes help me grow.
47. I enjoy challenges.
48. I stay consistent.
49. I am becoming fluent.
50. My confidence is growing.

# 🎓 60 Days Spoken English Master Course

# 🚀 Day 51: Advanced Pronunciation, Stress & Intonation (Speak Like a Native)

আজকের লক্ষ্য:

* 🔊 English pronunciation উন্নত করা
* 🎯 Word Stress (কোন syllable-এ জোর দিতে হবে)
* 🎵 Sentence Stress (বাক্যে কোন শব্দে জোর দিতে হবে)
* 🌊 Connected Speech (Native speakers কীভাবে শব্দ জোড়া লাগিয়ে বলেন)
* 🗣️ Intonation (কণ্ঠস্বরের উঠানামা)
* 🎤 Clear, confident, and natural English speaking

---

# 🎯 Lesson 1: Pronunciation Rules

বাংলা উচ্চারণে English বললে অনেক সময় বোঝা কঠিন হয়।

### ❌ Incorrect

* Iskool
* Istudent
* Espacially

### ✅ Correct

* School /skuːl/
* Student /ˈstjuːdənt/
* Especially /ɪˈspeʃəli/

---

## Practice

Say aloud:

* School
* Student
* Strong
* Street
* Spring
* Strategy
* Smile
* Speak
* Smart
* Success

---

# 🎯 Lesson 2: Word Stress

English-এ প্রতিটি শব্দের একটি stressed syllable থাকে।

## Examples

| Word           | Stress          |
| -------------- | --------------- |
| TAble          | **TA**-ble      |
| DOCtor         | **DOC**-tor     |
| WINdow         | **WIN**-dow     |
| imPORtant      | im-**POR**-tant |
| beGIN          | be-**GIN**      |
| sucCESS        | suc-**CESS**    |
| preSENT (verb) | pre-**SENT**    |
| PREsent (noun) | **PRE**-sent    |
| comPUter       | com-**PU**-ter  |
| toMORrow       | to-**MOR**-row  |

### Practice

Read these aloud five times:

* Important
* Computer
* Development
* Opportunity
* Communication

---

# 🎯 Lesson 3: Sentence Stress

সব শব্দে সমান জোর দেওয়া হয় না।

### Example

❌ I AM GOING TO THE MARKET TODAY.

### ✅

I am going to the **MARKET** **TODAY**.

আরও উদাহরণ:

* I **LOVE** learning English.
* She **BOUGHT** a new laptop.
* We are **READY** for the meeting.
* He **WORKS** very hard.
* This project is **IMPORTANT**.

---

# 🎯 Lesson 4: Intonation (Voice Movement)

## Rising Intonation ⬆️

ব্যবহার:

* Yes/No Questions

Examples:

* Are you ready? ⬆️
* Do you like coffee? ⬆️
* Can you help me? ⬆️

---

## Falling Intonation ⬇️

ব্যবহার:

* Statements
* WH-Questions

Examples:

* My name is Atiar. ⬇️
* Where do you live? ⬇️
* What are you doing? ⬇️

---

# 🎯 Lesson 5: Connected Speech

Native speakers প্রতিটি শব্দ আলাদা করে বলেন না।

তারা শব্দগুলো connect করেন।

## Examples

Want to → Wanna

* I wanna learn English.

Going to → Gonna *(অনানুষ্ঠানিক কথ্য ভাষা)*

* I'm gonna call you.

Give me → Gimme *(খুব অনানুষ্ঠানিক)*

* Gimme a minute.

Let me → Lemme

* Lemme explain.

Got to → Gotta

* I gotta go.

> **নোট:** এগুলো casual spoken English-এর জন্য। Formal presentation বা interview-এ পূর্ণ রূপ (want to, going to, give me) ব্যবহার করাই ভালো।

---

# 🎯 Lesson 6: Common Pronunciation Mistakes

| Wrong          | Correct                                           |
| -------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| Com-for-table  | Comfortable (ˈkʌmf-tər-bəl)                       |
| Ve-ge-ta-ble   | Vegetable (VEJ-tə-bəl)                            |
| Feb-ru-a-ry    | February (FEB-roo-er-ee)                          |
| Li-bra-ry      | Library (LAI-brer-ee)                             |
| Cho-co-late    | Chocolate (CHOK-lit / CHAWK-lət, accent অনুযায়ী) |
| In-te-res-ting | Interesting (IN-trəs-ting)                        |

---

# 🎤 Speaking Drill (Read Slowly)

Read this paragraph aloud **three times**.

> Good morning everyone. My name is Atiar Rahman. I am learning English because I want to become a confident software engineer. Every day I practice speaking, listening, reading, and writing. I know that improvement takes time, but I never give up. I believe consistency is the key to success.

---

# 🎧 Shadowing Exercise

Listen to an English speaker (YouTube, podcast, or movie).

Follow this process:

1. Listen to one sentence.
2. Pause.
3. Repeat exactly like the speaker.
4. Copy their pronunciation, stress, and intonation.
5. Record yourself and compare.

Practice for **10–15 minutes daily**.

---

## Writing

Write **15 sentences** using today's pronunciation words.

---

## Speaking Practice (5–7 minutes)

Read the paragraph above three times:

* First: Slow speed
* Second: Normal speed
* Third: Natural conversation speed

Record yourself and check:

* ✅ Clear pronunciation
* ✅ Correct word stress
* ✅ Natural sentence stress
* ✅ Smooth intonation
